## 1. PROJECT VISION & PHILOSOPHY

### What Is This?

`ishu.fun/tools` is a **world-class PDF & document utility platform** that combines:
- The **tool depth** of iLovePDF (120+ real working tools)
- The **design quality** of Linear / Vercel (dark glassmorphism, micro-animations)
- The **UX smoothness** of Figma / Framer (cursor effects, spring physics)
- The **performance** of Vercel Edge (< 1.2s LCP globally)
- The **3D richness** of Apple.com / Lusion.co / Three.js showcase sites
- The **SEO power** of a #1-ranking utility site

### Core Philosophy (NON-NEGOTIABLE)

```
вң… EVERY TOOL MUST WORK IN PRODUCTION вҖ” no fake UI, no placeholders
вң… EVERY ANIMATION MUST RUN AT 60fps вҖ” no janky scroll, no layout shift
вң… EVERY TOOL HAS ITS OWN ROUTE вҖ” /tools/merge-pdf, /tools/ocr-pdf etc.
вң… EVERY PAGE IS FULLY RESPONSIVE вҖ” pixel-perfect from 320px to 4K
вң… EVERY UPLOAD IS SECURE вҖ” MIME validation, virus scan, auto-delete
вң… SPEED IS A FEATURE вҖ” LCP < 1.2s, no blocking scripts, lazy everything
вң… DESIGN IS A FEATURE вҖ” Lucide/Phosphor icons ONLY (no AI-generated icons)
вң… SEO IS A FEATURE вҖ” rank #1 for every tool keyword
вң… REAL DATA ONLY вҖ” no fake stats, no placeholder text in production
вң… MOBILE-FIRST вҖ” every interaction works on touch/mobile
```

### Design Inspiration Matrix

| Source | What We Steal |
|--------|---------------|
| **Vercel.com** | Dark glassmorphism nav, grid cards, velocity feel |
| **Linear.app** | Keyboard shortcuts, smooth transitions, command palette, focus mode |
| **Stripe.com** | Gradient mesh backgrounds, scroll-reveal animations, trust signals |
| **Apple.com** | 3D product showcases, whitespace mastery, bold typography |
| **Framer.com** | Cursor follower, hover effects, visual density, motion choreography |
| **Figma.com** | Category sidebar, icon system, search bar UX, organized grid |
| **Notion.so** | Clean card hierarchy, tags, contextual menus |
| **GitHub.com** | Code clarity, dark theme excellence, information density |
| **Lusion.co** | Three.js 3D backgrounds, GPU-accelerated particles |
| **Raycast.com** | Command palette design, keyboard-first UX |
| **Resend.com** | Minimal dark aesthetic, crisp typography |
| **iLovePDF** | Tool card patterns, category grouping, upload UX |
| **Smallpdf** | Progress UX, result download flow, step indicators |
| **Adobe Acrobat** | Trust signals, premium feel, professional UI depth |
| **Clerk.com** | Component polish, micro-interaction quality |
| **Planetscale.com** | Dark mode excellence, developer-focused UI |

### 2.1 вҖ” Color Palette (CSS Custom Properties)

```css
/* styles/tokens.css */
:root {
  /* в”Җв”Җв”Җ BACKGROUNDS в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ */

  --color-bg-glass-hover:  rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.065);
  --color-bg-glass-active: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.10);

  /* в”Җв”Җв”Җ TEXT в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ */

  --color-border-strong:   rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.14);
  --color-border-focus:    rgba(99, 102, 241, 0.6);

  /* в”Җв”Җв”Җ BRAND ACCENTS в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ */

                             #6366F120 0deg, #8B5CF620 72deg,

  --shadow-sm:             0 1px 3px rgba(0,0,0,0.4), 0 1px 2px rgba(0,0,0,0.3);

  /* в”Җв”Җв”Җ BLUR в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ */

  --blur-md:  blur(16px);
  --blur-lg:  blur(24px);

  --radius-xs: 4px;  --radius-sm: 6px;  --radius-md: 10px;

  --z-toast: 400;   --z-tooltip: 500; --z-cursor: 9999;
}

### 2.2 вҖ” Typography System

```css
/* Fonts loaded via next/font (zero FOUT) */

:root {
  --font-display:  'Plus Jakarta Sans', sans-serif;  /* Headlines */
  --font-heading:  'DM Serif Display', serif;         /* Hero text */
  --font-body:     'DM Sans', sans-serif;              /* Body copy */
  --font-mono:     'JetBrains Mono', monospace;        /* Code, badges */
  --font-ui:       'Plus Jakarta Sans', sans-serif;   /* UI elements */

  /* Fluid Type Scale (clamp) */
  --text-xs:   clamp(10px, 1vw + 8px, 12px);
  --text-sm:   clamp(12px, 1vw + 10px, 14px);
  --text-base: clamp(14px, 1vw + 12px, 16px);
  --text-lg:   clamp(16px, 1.5vw + 12px, 18px);
  --text-xl:   clamp(18px, 2vw + 12px, 22px);
  --text-2xl:  clamp(22px, 3vw + 12px, 28px);
  --text-3xl:  clamp(28px, 4vw + 14px, 40px);
  --text-4xl:  clamp(36px, 5vw + 16px, 56px);
  --text-5xl:  clamp(48px, 7vw + 16px, 80px);
  --text-6xl:  clamp(64px, 9vw + 16px, 112px);
}
```

## 3. TECH STACK вҖ” FRONTEND

### 3.1 вҖ” Core Framework & Build

```
Framework:       Next.js 15 (App Router + Partial Prerendering)
Language:        TypeScript 5.5 (strict mode, all checks enabled)
Styling:         Tailwind CSS v4 (Oxide engine) + CSS Modules + CSS Variables
Package Manager: pnpm 9.x (workspaces, turbo cache)
Bundler:         Turbopack (700% faster HMR than webpack)
Node Version:    22 LTS
```

### 3.2 вҖ” UI Component Libraries

```
shadcn/ui v2      вҖ” Headless, copy-owned components (Button, Dialog, Tabs, etc.)
Radix UI          вҖ” Accessible primitives (tooltips, dropdowns, popovers)
Lucide React      вҖ” 1500+ SVG icons (tree-shakeable, consistent stroke width)
Phosphor Icons    вҖ” Duotone variants for tool card icons
react-icons       вҖ” Extended icon fallback (brand icons, etc.)
```

### 3.3 вҖ” Animation Libraries (ALL ACTIVE IN PRODUCTION)

```
GSAP 3.12 + ScrollTrigger + SplitText + DrawSVG + MorphSVG + CustomEase
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ ScrollTrigger      Scroll-based animations, pinning, scrub parallax
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ ScrollSmoother     Native-feel smooth scroll
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ SplitText          Char/word/line text splitting for hero reveals
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ DrawSVGPlugin      SVG path draw-on animations (upload icon)
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ MorphSVGPlugin     Shape morphing between states
  в””в”Җв”Җ CustomEase         Designer easing curves

Framer Motion 11 (motion/react)
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ AnimatePresence    Mount/unmount transitions
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ useScroll          Scroll-linked progress values
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ useSpring          Physics-based spring animations
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ layoutId           Shared layout transitions (magic move)
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Reorder            Drag-to-reorder file lists
  в””в”Җв”Җ useMotionValue     Cursor follower, card 3D tilt

Three.js r168 + React Three Fiber + Drei
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ @react-three/fiber       JSX renderer for Three.js
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ @react-three/drei        Float, Environment, Sparkles, Text3D
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ @react-three/postprocessing  Bloom, ChromaticAberration
  в””в”Җв”Җ @react-three/rapier      Physics engine for 3D elements

Anime.js 4.x
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ SVG path animations (upload zone icon morphing)
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Staggered element entry reveals
  в””в”Җв”Җ Number ticker/counter effects

React Spring 9.x
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Physics-based card hover (tilt + scale)
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Progress bar spring transitions
  в””в”Җв”Җ Modal entrance/exit physics

Lenis 1.3 (smooth scroll)
  в””в”Җв”Җ Ultra-smooth momentum scrolling synced with GSAP ScrollTrigger

Barba.js 2.x (page transitions)
  в””в”Җв”Җ SPA-feel route transitions with GSAP timeline hooks

AutoAnimate 0.8
  в””в”Җв”Җ Zero-config list/grid auto-animations (file list reordering)

Motion One (Web Animations API wrapper)
  в””в”Җв”Җ CSS animation performance layer for non-JS fallback

velocity-animate 2.x
  в””в”Җв”Җ DOM animation fallback for lower-end devices

react-intersection-observer
  в””в”Җв”Җ Efficient viewport detection for scroll-triggered animations

Typed.js 2.x
  в””в”Җв”Җ Hero section typewriter cycling effect

  в””в”Җв”Җ Animated stat counters (50M+ files processed, etc.)

  в””в”Җв”Җ Multi-layer depth parallax scrolling

  в””в”Җв”Җ SVG morphing and CSS property tweening

  в””в”Җв”Җ Mouse-follow 3D tilt on tool cards (gyroscope on mobile)

## 4. TECH STACK вҖ” BACKEND

### 4.1 вҖ” Runtime & Framework

```
Runtime:    Node.js 22 LTS
Framework:  Fastify 5.x (2x faster than Express, native TypeScript)
Language:   TypeScript 5.5 (strict mode)
Validation: Zod 3.x + @fastify/type-provider-zod
Process:    Cluster mode with PM2 for multi-core utilization
```

### 4.2 вҖ” PDF Processing Engines

```
pdf-lib 1.17.x
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Merge, split, rotate, protect, watermark, page numbers
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Add text, images, signatures, form field filling
  в””в”Җв”Җ Metadata read/write, page resize, PDF/A conversion

@pdf-lib/fontkit     Custom font embedding in PDFs
pdf2json             Text/data extraction from PDFs
pdfjs-dist           Server-side PDF rendering + text extraction
hummus-recipe        Advanced PDF manipulation
pdf-merger-js        Alternative merge engine
qpdf (CLI)           High-performance PDF linearization + encryption
poppler-utils (CLI)  pdftotext, pdftoppm, pdfinfo
ghostscript (CLI)    PDF compression, PS conversion, color correction
libvips + sharp      Ultra-fast image extraction and conversion
pdfcpu (Go binary)   Ultra-fast microservice for bulk operations
```

### 4.3 вҖ” Document Conversion

```
LibreOffice 7.6 (headless)   DOC/DOCX/XLS/XLSX/PPT/PPTX/ODT/ODS вҶ’ PDF

mammoth 1.x                  DOCX вҶ’ HTML/Markdown

pptxgenjs 3.x                Generate PowerPoint programmatically
officegen                    Generate DOCX, XLSX, PPTX from scratch
marked 9.x                   Markdown вҶ’ HTML pipeline
turndown 7.x                 HTML вҶ’ Markdown
calibre (CLI)                EPUB/MOBI/AZW3/FB2 conversions
imagemagick 7.x (CLI)        BMP/TIFF/GIF/HEIC, DPI control
heic-convert                 Node.js HEIC/HEIF conversion
img2pdf (Python bridge)      Image вҶ’ PDF via subprocess
```

### 4.4 вҖ” OCR Engine

```
tesseract.js 5.x
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ 100+ languages (all major Indian languages)
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ LSTM neural network engine (highest accuracy)
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Worker pool for concurrent processing
  в””в”Җв”Җ Returns searchable PDF or plain text

node-tesseract-ocr   CLI wrapper (faster for large documents)
```

### 4.5 вҖ” AI/ML Features

```
OpenAI SDK 4.x       GPT-4o: Summarize PDF, Translate PDF
Anthropic SDK 0.26.x Claude: Chat with PDF (RAG), AI analysis
LangChain.js 0.2.x   RAG pipeline for Chat with PDF
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ RecursiveCharacterTextSplitter (chunk PDF text)
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ OpenAI text-embedding-3-small (vector embeddings)
  в””в”Җв”Җ FAISS in-memory vector store (per session, auto-cleanup)
```

### 4.6 вҖ” File & Archive Handling

```
archiver 7.x         Create ZIP files (for batch image downloads)
node-stream-zip      Extract ZIP archives
multer 1.x           Multipart file upload middleware
multer-s3            Direct stream to Cloudflare R2/S3
busboy               Low-level multipart parser
file-type 19.x       Binary MIME type sniffing (security)
magic-bytes.js       Alternative binary signature detection
p-queue              Concurrency-controlled promise queue
p-limit              Limit concurrent file operations
stream-buffers       Memory-efficient Buffer streaming
```

### 4.7 вҖ” Queue & Job Processing

```
BullMQ 5.x (primary queue вҖ” Redis-backed)
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ PDF jobs queue (priority: pro > free users)
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ OCR jobs queue (separate worker pool)
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Convert jobs queue (LibreOffice/Puppeteer heavy)
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ AI jobs queue (rate-limited by API tokens)
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Retry: 3 attempts, exponential backoff (1s, 4s, 16s)
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Dead-letter queue for persistent failures
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Job events: active, progress, completed, failed
  в””в”Җв”Җ Stalled job detection and auto-recovery

bull-board 6.x       Admin UI at /admin/queues for queue monitoring
```

### 4.8 вҖ” Authentication & Authorization

```
NextAuth.js v5 (Auth.js)
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Google OAuth 2.0
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ GitHub OAuth
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Email magic link (via Resend)
  в””в”Җв”Җ WhatsApp number verification (Twilio)

jsonwebtoken 9.x     API JWT signing (RS256 algorithm)
argon2               Modern password hashing (time-constant)
RBAC system          Roles: guest | user | pro | admin
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ guest: 3 files/day, max 25MB/file
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ user:  15 files/day, max 50MB/file
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ pro:   unlimited, max 300MB/file, priority queue
  в””в”Җв”Җ admin: full access + admin panel
```

### 4.9 вҖ” Storage Services

```
Cloudflare R2 (primary storage)
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ S3-compatible API вҖ” zero egress fees
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Temp uploads: auto-delete after 1 hour
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Output files: auto-delete after 24 hours
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ CDN delivery via Cloudflare edge network
  в””в”Җв”Җ Pre-signed URLs for secure downloads

@aws-sdk/client-s3   SDK for R2/S3 operations
multer-s3            Direct multipart stream to R2
```

### 4.10 вҖ” Notifications

```
Twilio WhatsApp Business API
  в””в”Җв”Җ "Your file is ready! Download link: ..." after processing

Resend               Transactional emails (magic links, receipts)
nodemailer           Fallback SMTP email sending
web-push             Browser push notifications (PWA, requires permission)
```

### 4.11 вҖ” Security & API Hardening

```
@fastify/helmet      Security headers (CSP, HSTS, X-Frame-Options)
@fastify/cors        CORS: only ishu.fun origin allowed in production
@fastify/rate-limit  Rate limiting: 150 req/15min (global), 15 uploads/min
fastify-csrf         CSRF tokens for stateful POST operations
file-type 19.x       Binary MIME sniffing (prevent polyglot attacks)
ClamAV (clamdjs)     Async virus scanning of uploaded files
hpp                  HTTP parameter pollution prevention
```

### 4.12 вҖ” Logging & Observability

```
pino 9.x             Structured JSON logging (Fastify native)
pino-pretty          Human-readable dev logs with color
@opentelemetry/sdk   Distributed tracing (exports to Grafana/Jaeger)
Sentry Node.js SDK   Error tracking + performance monitoring
prom-client          Prometheus /metrics endpoint
clinic.js            Node.js profiling (flame graphs)
```

## 5. TECH STACK вҖ” DATABASE & CACHE

### 5.1 вҖ” Primary Database

```
PostgreSQL 16
  Provider:    Supabase (managed, built-in auth, realtime)
  Alternative: Neon (serverless, branching for dev)
  Connection:  PgBouncer pool (max 100 connections)

Prisma 5.x (ORM)
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Type-safe queries (full TypeScript inference)
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Prisma Migrate (schema versioning)
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Prisma Studio (visual DB admin)
  в””в”Җв”Җ Prisma Accelerate (global query caching)
```

### 5.2 вҖ” Cache & Sessions

```
Redis (via Upstash вҖ” serverless, pay-per-use)
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ BullMQ job queue backend
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Job status caching (TTL: 1 hour)
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Rate limit counters (sliding window)
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Tool list response cache (TTL: 5 min)
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Session tokens
  в””в”Җв”Җ Temp file metadata (size, mime, expiry)

ioredis              Redis client for Node.js
```

### 5.3 вҖ” Database Schema (Production)

```sql
-- в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
-- USERS
-- в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
CREATE TABLE users (
  id              UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  email           TEXT UNIQUE,
  name            TEXT,
  avatar_url      TEXT,
  whatsapp_no     TEXT,
  auth_provider   TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'email',
  role            TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'user'
                    CHECK (role IN ('user','pro','admin')),
  plan            TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'free'
                    CHECK (plan IN ('free','pro','enterprise')),
  plan_expires    TIMESTAMPTZ,
  daily_quota     INTEGER DEFAULT 3,
  daily_used      INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  daily_reset_at  TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  notify_whatsapp BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  notify_email    BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
  created_at      TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  updated_at      TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
-- FILE PROCESSING JOBS
-- в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
CREATE TABLE file_jobs (
  id                UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  bull_job_id       TEXT UNIQUE,
  tool_slug         TEXT NOT NULL,
  user_id           UUID REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  ip_hash           TEXT,
  status            TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'queued'
                      CHECK (status IN ('queued','active','completed','failed','cancelled')),
  input_r2_keys     TEXT[] NOT NULL DEFAULT '{}',
  output_r2_key     TEXT,
  file_sizes_bytes  BIGINT[] DEFAULT '{}',
  output_size_bytes BIGINT,
  page_count        INTEGER,
  processing_ms     INTEGER,
  options           JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
  error_message     TEXT,
  expires_at        TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW() + INTERVAL '24 hours',
  created_at        TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  completed_at      TIMESTAMPTZ
);

-- в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
-- TOOL USAGE ANALYTICS
-- в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
CREATE TABLE tool_usage (
  id                UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  tool_slug         TEXT NOT NULL,
  user_id           UUID REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  ip_hash           TEXT,
  file_size_bytes   BIGINT,
  output_size_bytes BIGINT,
  processing_ms     INTEGER,
  status            TEXT,
  country_code      TEXT,
  ua_browser        TEXT,
  ua_os             TEXT,
  created_at        TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
-- TOOLS CONFIGURATION (Admin-controlled)
-- в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
CREATE TABLE tools_config (
  id          UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  slug        TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL,
  name        TEXT NOT NULL,
  category    TEXT NOT NULL,
  description TEXT,
  is_active   BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
  is_new      BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  is_beta     BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  is_premium  BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  is_popular  BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  icon_name   TEXT,
  sort_order  INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  daily_uses  INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  created_at  TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  updated_at  TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
-- PERFORMANCE INDEXES
-- в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
CREATE INDEX idx_file_jobs_user_id    ON file_jobs(user_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_file_jobs_status     ON file_jobs(status);
CREATE INDEX idx_file_jobs_created    ON file_jobs(created_at DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_file_jobs_expires    ON file_jobs(expires_at);
CREATE INDEX idx_tool_usage_slug      ON tool_usage(tool_slug);
CREATE INDEX idx_tool_usage_created   ON tool_usage(created_at DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_tools_config_slug    ON tools_config(slug);
CREATE INDEX idx_tools_config_cat     ON tools_config(category);
CREATE INDEX idx_users_email          ON users(email);
CREATE INDEX idx_users_whatsapp       ON users(whatsapp_no);
```

## 6. TECH STACK вҖ” DEVOPS & INFRASTRUCTURE

### 6.1 вҖ” Frontend Deployment (Vercel)

```yaml
Platform:    Vercel Pro
Domain:      ishu.fun вҶ’ /tools/* routes
Build:       next build (Turbopack, ~45s)
Runtime:     Edge + Node.js serverless functions
CDN:         Vercel Edge Network (100+ PoPs globally)
Analytics:   Vercel Analytics (CWV) + Speed Insights
Caching:     ISR for tool pages (revalidate: 3600s)
Preview:     Auto preview URL per PR

vercel.json:
{
  "buildCommand": "pnpm build",
  "framework": "nextjs",
  "headers": [
    {
      "source": "/(.*)",
      "headers": [
        { "key": "X-DNS-Prefetch-Control", "value": "on" },
        { "key": "Strict-Transport-Security",
          "value": "max-age=63072000; includeSubDomains; preload" },
        { "key": "X-Frame-Options", "value": "DENY" },
        { "key": "X-Content-Type-Options", "value": "nosniff" },
        { "key": "Referrer-Policy",
          "value": "strict-origin-when-cross-origin" },
        { "key": "Permissions-Policy",
          "value": "camera=(), microphone=(), geolocation=()" }
      ]
    }
  ]
}
```

### 6.2 вҖ” Backend Deployment (Render)

```yaml
# render.yaml
services:
  - type: web
    name: ishu-tools-api
    env: node
    plan: standard          # $25/mo вҖ” always-on, no cold starts
    region: oregon
    buildCommand: pnpm install && pnpm build
    startCommand: node dist/server.js
    healthCheckPath: /health
    autoDeploy: true

  - type: worker
    name: ishu-pdf-worker
    env: node
    plan: standard
    startCommand: node dist/workers/pdf.worker.js
    envVars:
      - key: WORKER_CONCURRENCY
        value: "3"

  - type: worker
    name: ishu-ocr-worker
    env: node
    plan: standard
    startCommand: node dist/workers/ocr.worker.js

  - type: worker
    name: ishu-convert-worker
    env: node
    plan: standard
    startCommand: node dist/workers/convert.worker.js

databases:
  - name: ishu-db
    databaseName: ishu_tools
    user: ishu
    plan: starter
```

### 6.3 вҖ” CI/CD Pipeline (GitHub Actions)

```yaml
# .github/workflows/ci-cd.yml
name: CI/CD

on:
  push:    { branches: [main] }
  pull_request: { branches: [main] }

jobs:
  quality:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - uses: pnpm/action-setup@v4
      - uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with: { node-version: 22 }
      - run: pnpm install --frozen-lockfile
      - run: pnpm type-check
      - run: pnpm lint
      - run: pnpm test:unit
      - run: pnpm test:integration

  lighthouse:
    needs: quality
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: treosh/lighthouse-ci-action@v11
        with:
          urls: "https://preview-${{ github.sha }}.vercel.app/tools"
          budgetPath: "./.lighthouserc.json"

  deploy:
    needs: quality
    if: github.ref == 'refs/heads/main'
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - run: pnpm build
      - name: Deploy Frontend
        run: vercel --prod --token=${{ secrets.VERCEL_TOKEN }}
      - name: Deploy Backend
        run: curl -X POST ${{ secrets.RENDER_DEPLOY_HOOK }}
      - name: Notify Sentry Release
        run: sentry-cli releases finalize ${{ github.sha }}
```

### 6.4 вҖ” Infrastructure Services

```
Database:     Supabase (PostgreSQL 16) вҖ” supabase.com
Cache/Queue:  Upstash Redis вҖ” pay-per-use serverless
Storage:      Cloudflare R2 вҖ” zero egress, global CDN
Email:        Resend вҖ” 100/day free, simple API
WhatsApp:     Twilio WhatsApp Business API
Error:        Sentry вҖ” error + performance tracking
Analytics:    PostHog (self-hosted or cloud)
CDN/DNS:      Cloudflare вҖ” DNS, DDoS protection, WAF
SSL:          Cloudflare automatic SSL (full strict mode)
Secrets:      Doppler (dev) + Vercel/Render env vars (prod)
Uptime:       BetterStack (heartbeat checks every 1 min)
```

### Tool TypeScript Interface

```typescript
// packages/tool-registry/src/types.ts

export interface ToolOption {
  id: string;
  type: 'slider' | 'select' | 'toggle' | 'range' | 'text' | 'color' | 'number';
  label: string;
  description?: string;
  default: any;
  min?: number;
  max?: number;
  step?: number;
  unit?: string;              // "px", "mm", "DPI" etc.
  options?: { label: string; value: string; icon?: string }[];
  showWhen?: { field: string; value: any };  // conditional visibility
}

export interface Tool {
  slug: string;
  name: string;
  shortName: string;
  description: string;
  longDescription: string;
  category: ToolCategory;
  icon: string;               // Lucide icon name
  iconPhosphor?: string;      // Phosphor icon for duotone variant
  color: string;              // Primary accent hex
  gradientClass: string;      // Tailwind gradient class
  inputFormats: string[];
  outputFormat: string;
  maxFileSizeMB: number;
  maxFiles: number;
  estimatedTimeSec: number;
  options: ToolOption[];
  isNew?: boolean;
  isBeta?: boolean;
  isPremium?: boolean;
  isPopular?: boolean;
  backendProcessor: string;
  relatedTools: string[];
  keywords: string[];         // For SEO meta keywords + Fuse.js search
  faqs: { q: string; a: string }[];
  features: string[];         // For "Why use this tool" feature list
  useCases: string[];         // "Perfect for: contracts, resumes, reports..."
}
```

### Complete Tools List вҖ” 120+ Tools

```

PDF SECURITY (3 tools):
  protect-pdf         Password + restrict permissions (256-bit AES)
  unlock-pdf          Remove password (owner password required)
  sign-pdf            Electronic signature (draw/type/upload)

EDIT PDF (12 tools):
  edit-pdf            Full editor (text, images, shapes)
  watermark-pdf       Text/image watermarks (opacity, angle, color)
  annotate-pdf        Sticky notes, comments, freehand drawings
  page-numbers-pdf    Custom page numbers (position, format)
  header-footer-pdf   Custom headers/footers
  redact-pdf          Permanently remove sensitive content
  grayscale-pdf       Convert color to black & white
  whiteout-pdf        Cover areas with white rectangles
  pdf-filler          Fill interactive PDF forms
  highlight-pdf       Highlight/underline/strikethrough (8 colors)
  flatten-pdf         Merge layers/annotations into static PDF
  add-text-pdf        Add text boxes anywhere on pages

EXTRACT & MANAGE (7 tools):
  extract-pages       Pull out specific pages
  extract-text        Export all text (TXT/DOCX, OCR for scanned)
  extract-images      Get all embedded images as ZIP
  edit-metadata       View/edit title, author, keywords, date
  remove-metadata     Strip all metadata for privacy
  create-pdf          Create blank PDF from scratch
  resize-pages        Resize to A4, Letter, A3, A5, custom

AI-POWERED (4 tools):
  ocr-pdf             Scanned вҶ’ searchable (100+ languages, LSTM)
  translate-pdf       AI translation to 50+ languages
  summarize-pdf       AI summary (bullet points or paragraph)
  chat-with-pdf       RAG-powered Q&A with page citations

ADVANCED (4 tools):
  compare-pdf         Side-by-side diff (red/green highlighting)
  scan-to-pdf         Phone camera вҶ’ PDF (auto-enhance, deskew)
  pdf-viewer          In-browser viewer (zoom, search, navigate)
  repair-pdf          Fix corrupted PDFs
```

## 1. PROJECT VISION & PHILOSOPHY

### What Is This?

`ishu.fun/tools` is a **world-class PDF & document utility platform** that combines:
- The **tool depth** of iLovePDF (100+ real working tools)
- The **design quality** of Linear / Vercel (dark glassmorphism, micro-animations)
- The **UX smoothness** of Figma / Framer (cursor effects, spring physics)
- The **performance** of Vercel Edge (< 1.2s LCP globally)
- The **3D richness** of Apple.com / Three.js showcase sites
- The **SEO power** of a #1-ranking utility site

### Core Philosophy (NON-NEGOTIABLE)

```
вң… EVERY TOOL MUST WORK IN PRODUCTION вҖ” no fake UI, no placeholders
вң… EVERY ANIMATION MUST RUN AT 60fps вҖ” no janky scroll, no layout shift
вң… EVERY TOOL HAS ITS OWN ROUTE вҖ” /tools/merge-pdf, /tools/ocr-pdf etc.
вң… EVERY PAGE IS FULLY RESPONSIVE вҖ” pixel-perfect from 320px to 4K
вң… EVERY UPLOAD IS SECURE вҖ” MIME validation, virus scan, auto-delete
вң… SPEED IS A FEATURE вҖ” LCP < 1.2s, no blocking scripts, lazy everything
вң… DESIGN IS A FEATURE вҖ” Lucide/Phosphor icons ONLY (no AI-generated)
вң… SEO IS A FEATURE вҖ” rank #1 for every tool keyword
```

### Design Inspiration Matrix

| Source | What We Steal |
|--------|---------------|
| **Vercel.com** | Dark glassmorphism nav, grid cards, velocity feel |
| **Linear.app** | Keyboard shortcuts, smooth transitions, command palette, focus mode |
| **Stripe.com** | Gradient mesh backgrounds, scroll-reveal animations, trust signals |
| **Apple.com** | 3D product showcases, whitespace mastery, bold typography |
| **Framer.com** | Cursor follower, hover effects, visual density, motion choreography |
| **Figma.com** | Category sidebar, icon system, search bar UX, organized grid |
| **Notion.so** | Clean card hierarchy, tags, contextual menus |
| **GitHub.com** | Code clarity, dark theme excellence, information density |
| **Lusion.co** | Three.js 3D backgrounds, GPU-accelerated particles |
| **iLovePDF** | Tool card patterns, category grouping, upload UX |
| **Smallpdf** | Progress UX, result download flow, step indicators |
| **Adobe Acrobat** | Trust signals, premium feel, professional UI depth |
| **Raycast.com** | Command palette design, keyboard-first UX |
| **Resend.com** | Minimal dark aesthetic, crisp typography |
| **Clerk.com** | Component polish, micro-interaction quality |

## 2. DESIGN SYSTEM

### 2.1 вҖ” Color Palette (CSS Custom Properties)

```css
/* styles/tokens.css */
:root {
  /* в”Җв”Җв”Җ BACKGROUNDS в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ */

  --color-bg-surface:     #0D0D1A;   /* Cards, panels */
  --color-bg-elevated:    #12121F;   /* Dropdowns, modals */
  --color-bg-overlay:     #1A1A2E;   /* Hover states, subtle depth */
  --color-bg-glass:       rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.03);
  --color-bg-glass-hover: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.065);
  --color-bg-glass-active:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.10);

  /* в”Җв”Җв”Җ TEXT в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ */

  /* в”Җв”Җв”Җ BORDERS в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ */

  --gradient-card-green:  linear-gradient(135deg, rgba(16,185,129,0.15) 0%, rgba(6,182,212,0.08) 100%);
  --gradient-card-purple: linear-gradient(135deg, rgba(139,92,246,0.15) 0%, rgba(236,72,153,0.08) 100%);
  --gradient-card-amber:  linear-gradient(135deg, rgba(245,158,11,0.15) 0%, rgba(249,115,22,0.08) 100%);

  /* в”Җв”Җв”Җ SHADOWS в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ */

  --duration-slow:   350ms;
  --duration-slower: 500ms;

  /* в”Җв”Җв”Җ Z-INDEX SCALE в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ */
  --z-below: -1;    --z-base: 0;     --z-raised: 10;
  --z-dropdown: 100; --z-sticky: 200; --z-modal: 300;
  --z-toast: 400;   --z-tooltip: 500; --z-cursor: 9999;
}
```

### 2.2 вҖ” Typography System

```css
/* Fonts loaded via next/font (zero FOUT) */

/* PRIMARY DISPLAY вҖ” Bold, Geometric, Impact */
/* "Plus Jakarta Sans" вҖ” modern alternative to Satoshi */
/* Weight: 700, 800 for headlines */

/* SECONDARY вҖ” Strong, Editorial */
/* "DM Serif Display" вҖ” for large hero text with character */

/* BODY вҖ” Clean, Readable */
/* "DM Sans" вҖ” versatile, friendly at all sizes */

/* MONO вҖ” Technical */
/* "JetBrains Mono" вҖ” code, tags, badges */

:root {
  --font-display:  'Plus Jakarta Sans', sans-serif;
  --font-heading:  'DM Serif Display', serif;
  --font-body:     'DM Sans', sans-serif;
  --font-mono:     'JetBrains Mono', monospace;
  --font-ui:       'Plus Jakarta Sans', sans-serif;

  /* Type Scale вҖ” Fluid (clamp-based) */
  --text-xs:   clamp(10px, 1vw + 8px, 12px);
  --text-sm:   clamp(12px, 1vw + 10px, 14px);
  --text-base: clamp(14px, 1vw + 12px, 16px);
  --text-lg:   clamp(16px, 1.5vw + 12px, 18px);
  --text-xl:   clamp(18px, 2vw + 12px, 22px);
  --text-2xl:  clamp(22px, 3vw + 12px, 28px);
  --text-3xl:  clamp(28px, 4vw + 14px, 40px);
  --text-4xl:  clamp(36px, 5vw + 16px, 56px);
  --text-5xl:  clamp(48px, 7vw + 16px, 80px);
  --text-6xl:  clamp(64px, 9vw + 16px, 112px);
}

/* Typography Utility Classes */
.text-display {
  font-family: var(--font-display);
  font-weight: 800;
  letter-spacing: -0.03em;
  line-height: 1.05;
}

.text-heading {
  font-family: var(--font-heading);
  font-weight: 700;
  letter-spacing: -0.02em;
  line-height: 1.1;
}

.text-body {
  font-family: var(--font-body);
  font-weight: 400;
  letter-spacing: -0.01em;
  line-height: 1.6;
}

.gradient-text {
  background: var(--gradient-brand);
  -webkit-background-clip: text;
  -webkit-text-fill-color: transparent;
  background-clip: text;
}
```

## 5. TECH STACK вҖ” DATABASE & CACHE

### 5.1 вҖ” Primary Database

```
PostgreSQL 16
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Provider: Supabase (managed, free вҶ’ Pro вҶ’ Enterprise)
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Alternative: Neon (serverless PostgreSQL, branching)
  в””в”Җв”Җ Connection: PgBouncer connection pooling

Prisma 5.x (ORM)
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Type-safe queries (full TypeScript inference)
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Prisma Migrate (schema versioning)
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Prisma Studio (visual DB admin)
  в””в”Җв”Җ Prisma Accelerate (global connection pool, query cache)
```

### 5.2 вҖ” Cache & Sessions

```
Redis (via Upstash)
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ BullMQ queue backend
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Job status caching (poll every 1.5s)
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Rate limit counters
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Tool list response cache (TTL: 5min)
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Session store
  в””в”Җв”Җ Temp metadata (file size, tool used, expiry time)

ioredis                вҖ” Redis client for Node.js
```

### 5.3 вҖ” Database Schema (Complete)

```sql
-- в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
-- USERS
-- в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
CREATE TABLE users (
  id            UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  email         TEXT UNIQUE,
  name          TEXT,
  avatar_url    TEXT,
  whatsapp_no   TEXT,
  auth_provider TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'email',
  role          TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'user' CHECK (role IN ('user', 'pro', 'admin')),
  plan          TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'free' CHECK (plan IN ('free', 'pro', 'enterprise')),
  plan_expires  TIMESTAMPTZ,
  monthly_quota INTEGER DEFAULT 50,   -- files per month for free tier
  monthly_used  INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  notify_whatsapp BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  notify_email    BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
  created_at    TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  updated_at    TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
-- FILE PROCESSING JOBS
-- в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
CREATE TABLE file_jobs (
  id              UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  bull_job_id     TEXT UNIQUE,
  tool_slug       TEXT NOT NULL,
  user_id         UUID REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  ip_hash         TEXT,                      -- hashed IP for anonymous users
  status          TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'queued'
                    CHECK (status IN ('queued','active','completed','failed','cancelled')),
  input_r2_keys   TEXT[] NOT NULL DEFAULT '{}',
  output_r2_key   TEXT,
  file_sizes_bytes BIGINT[] DEFAULT '{}',
  output_size_bytes BIGINT,
  page_count      INTEGER,
  processing_ms   INTEGER,
  options         JSONB DEFAULT '{}',         -- tool-specific options (quality, range, etc.)
  error_message   TEXT,
  expires_at      TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW() + INTERVAL '24 hours',
  created_at      TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  completed_at    TIMESTAMPTZ
);

-- в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
-- TOOL USAGE ANALYTICS
-- в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
CREATE TABLE tool_usage (
  id              UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  tool_slug       TEXT NOT NULL,
  user_id         UUID REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  ip_hash         TEXT,
  file_size_bytes BIGINT,
  output_size_bytes BIGINT,
  processing_ms   INTEGER,
  status          TEXT,
  country_code    TEXT,
  user_agent      TEXT,
  created_at      TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
-- TOOLS CONFIGURATION (Admin-controlled)
-- в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
CREATE TABLE tools_config (
  id          UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  slug        TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL,
  name        TEXT NOT NULL,
  category    TEXT NOT NULL,
  description TEXT,
  is_active   BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
  is_new      BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  is_beta     BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  is_premium  BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  icon_name   TEXT,
  sort_order  INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  daily_uses  INTEGER DEFAULT 0,    -- cached from analytics
  created_at  TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  updated_at  TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
-- INDEXES
-- в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
CREATE INDEX idx_file_jobs_user_id ON file_jobs(user_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_file_jobs_status ON file_jobs(status);
CREATE INDEX idx_file_jobs_created_at ON file_jobs(created_at DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_tool_usage_slug ON tool_usage(tool_slug);
CREATE INDEX idx_tool_usage_created_at ON tool_usage(created_at DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_tools_config_slug ON tools_config(slug);
CREATE INDEX idx_tools_config_category ON tools_config(category);
```

## 6. TECH STACK вҖ” DEVOPS & INFRASTRUCTURE

### 6.1 вҖ” Frontend Deployment (Vercel)

```yaml
Platform:     Vercel Pro
Domain:       ishu.fun вҶ’ /tools/* routes
Build:        next build (Turbopack)
Runtime:      Edge + Node.js serverless
CDN:          Vercel Edge Network (100+ PoPs globally)
Analytics:    Vercel Analytics (CWV) + Vercel Speed Insights
Preview:      Automatic per-PR preview URLs
Caching:      ISR for tool pages (revalidate: 3600s)

vercel.json:
{
  "buildCommand": "pnpm build",
  "outputDirectory": ".next",
  "framework": "nextjs",
  "headers": [
    {
      "source": "/(.*)",
      "headers": [
        { "key": "X-DNS-Prefetch-Control", "value": "on" },
        { "key": "Strict-Transport-Security", "value": "max-age=63072000; includeSubDomains; preload" },
        { "key": "X-Frame-Options", "value": "DENY" },
        { "key": "X-Content-Type-Options", "value": "nosniff" },
        { "key": "Referrer-Policy", "value": "strict-origin-when-cross-origin" },
        { "key": "Permissions-Policy", "value": "camera=(), microphone=(), geolocation=()" }
      ]
    }
  ]
}
```

### 6.2 вҖ” Backend Deployment (Render)

```yaml
# render.yaml
services:
  # в”Җв”Җ API SERVER в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  - type: web
    name: ishu-tools-api
    env: node
    plan: standard          # $25/mo вҖ” always-on, no cold starts
    region: oregon          # us-west (closest to India + US)
    buildCommand: pnpm install && pnpm build
    startCommand: node dist/server.js
    healthCheckPath: /health
    autoDeploy: true
    envVars:
      - key: NODE_ENV
        value: production
      - key: PORT
        value: 3001
      - key: DATABASE_URL
        fromDatabase: { name: ishu-db, property: connectionString }
      - key: REDIS_URL
        sync: false
      - key: R2_ACCOUNT_ID
        sync: false
      # ... (see Section 25 for full list)

  # в”Җв”Җ PDF WORKER в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  - type: worker
    name: ishu-pdf-worker
    env: node
    plan: standard
    buildCommand: pnpm install && pnpm build
    startCommand: node dist/workers/pdf.worker.js
    envVars:
      - key: WORKER_CONCURRENCY
        value: "3"           # 3 parallel PDF jobs

  # в”Җв”Җ OCR WORKER в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  - type: worker
    name: ishu-ocr-worker
    env: node
    plan: standard
    startCommand: node dist/workers/ocr.worker.js

databases:
  - name: ishu-db
    databaseName: ishu_tools
    user: ishu
    plan: starter
```

### 6.3 вҖ” CI/CD Pipeline (GitHub Actions)

```yaml
# .github/workflows/ci-cd.yml
name: CI/CD Pipeline

on:
  push:
    branches: [main]
  pull_request:
    branches: [main]

jobs:
  quality:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - uses: pnpm/action-setup@v4
      - uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with: { node-version: 22 }
      - run: pnpm install --frozen-lockfile
      - run: pnpm type-check         # tsc --noEmit
      - run: pnpm lint               # ESLint + Prettier
      - run: pnpm test:unit          # Vitest unit tests
      - run: pnpm test:integration   # API integration tests

  build-and-deploy:
    needs: quality
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    if: github.ref == 'refs/heads/main'
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - run: pnpm build              # Turbopack build
      - name: Deploy Frontend
        run: vercel --prod --token=${{ secrets.VERCEL_TOKEN }}
      - name: Deploy Backend
        run: curl -X POST ${{ secrets.RENDER_DEPLOY_HOOK }}
```

### 6.4 вҖ” Infrastructure Services

```
Database:     Supabase (PostgreSQL 16) вҖ” supabase.com
Cache/Queue:  Upstash Redis вҖ” pay-per-use, serverless
Storage:      Cloudflare R2 вҖ” zero egress, global CDN
Email:        Resend вҖ” transactional email API
WhatsApp:     Twilio WhatsApp Business API
Monitoring:   Sentry (errors) + Datadog (APM) вҖ” or BetterStack
Analytics:    PostHog (self-hosted or cloud)
CDN/DNS:      Cloudflare (DNS, DDoS protection, WAF)
SSL:          Cloudflare automatic SSL
Secrets:      Vercel/Render environment variables + Doppler (optional)
```

## 8. TOOLS MASTER REGISTRY (120+ Tools)

```typescript
// packages/tool-registry/src/tools.ts
// в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
// SINGLE SOURCE OF TRUTH вҖ” ALL 120+ TOOLS
// в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ

export type ToolCategory =
  | 'organize'
  | 'convert-from-pdf'
  | 'convert-to-pdf'
  | 'pdf-security'
  | 'edit-pdf'
  | 'extract'
  | 'ai-powered'
  | 'advanced';

export interface ToolOption {
  id: string;
  type: 'slider' | 'select' | 'toggle' | 'range' | 'text' | 'color';
  label: string;
  description?: string;
  default: any;
  min?: number;
  max?: number;
  step?: number;
  options?: { label: string; value: string }[];
}

export interface Tool {
  slug: string;
  name: string;
  shortName: string;           // For mobile display
  description: string;         // 1-2 sentences
  longDescription: string;     // SEO paragraph
  category: ToolCategory;
  icon: string;                // Lucide icon name
  iconPhosphor?: string;       // Phosphor icon (duotone variant)
  color: string;               // Primary accent color
  gradientClass: string;       // Tailwind gradient class
  inputFormats: string[];
  outputFormat: string;
  maxFileSizeMB: number;
  maxFiles: number;            // Max files per operation
  estimatedTimeSec: number;    // UX estimate for progress UI
  options: ToolOption[];       // Tool-specific settings
  isNew?: boolean;
  isBeta?: boolean;
  isPremium?: boolean;
  isPopular?: boolean;
  backendProcessor: string;
  relatedTools: string[];
  keywords: string[];          // SEO keywords
  faqs: { q: string; a: string }[];
}

в”Ӯ   SEARCH BAR (scale-in, center):                                    в”Ӯ

## 10. INDIVIDUAL TOOL PAGE DESIGN

в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ RELATED TOOLS вҖ” horizontal scroll cards                             в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ "You might also need:"                                              в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ [Split PDF] [Compress PDF] [Organize PDF] [PDF to Word] ...        в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ

## 11. ANIMATION & MOTION DESIGN SYSTEM

### 11.1 вҖ” Complete CSS Keyframes Library

```css
/* в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
   styles/animations.css вҖ” Complete Keyframe Library
   в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ */

/* в”Җв”Җ ENTRANCE ANIMATIONS в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ */

@keyframes fade-up {
  from { opacity: 0; transform: translateY(24px); }
  to   { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0); }
}

@keyframes fade-down {
  from { opacity: 0; transform: translateY(-24px); }
  to   { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0); }
}

@keyframes fade-in {
  from { opacity: 0; }
  to   { opacity: 1; }
}

@keyframes scale-in {
  from { opacity: 0; transform: scale(0.92); }
  to   { opacity: 1; transform: scale(1); }
}

@keyframes slide-in-left {
  from { opacity: 0; transform: translateX(-32px); }
  to   { opacity: 1; transform: translateX(0); }
}

@keyframes slide-in-right {
  from { opacity: 0; transform: translateX(32px); }
  to   { opacity: 1; transform: translateX(0); }
}

/* в”Җв”Җ AMBIENT ANIMATIONS (infinite) в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ */

@keyframes float {
  0%, 100% { transform: translateY(0px) rotate(0deg); }
  33%       { transform: translateY(-12px) rotate(1deg); }
  66%       { transform: translateY(-6px) rotate(-1deg); }
}

@keyframes float-slow {
  0%, 100% { transform: translateY(0px); }
  50%       { transform: translateY(-20px); }
}

@keyframes pulse-glow {
  0%, 100% { box-shadow: 0 0 0 0 rgba(99,102,241,0.4), 0 0 20px rgba(99,102,241,0.2); }
  50%       { box-shadow: 0 0 0 12px rgba(99,102,241,0), 0 0 40px rgba(99,102,241,0.4); }
}

@keyframes border-glow {
  0%, 100% { border-color: rgba(99,102,241,0.2); box-shadow: none; }
  50%       { border-color: rgba(99,102,241,0.6); box-shadow: 0 0 20px rgba(99,102,241,0.2); }
}

@keyframes shimmer {
  from { background-position: -200% center; }
  to   { background-position: 200% center; }
}

@keyframes gradient-shift {
  0%   { background-position: 0% 50%; }
  50%  { background-position: 100% 50%; }
  100% { background-position: 0% 50%; }
}

@keyframes spin-slow {
  from { transform: rotate(0deg); }
  to   { transform: rotate(360deg); }
}

@keyframes ping {
  75%, 100% { transform: scale(2); opacity: 0; }
}

@keyframes marquee {
  from { transform: translateX(0); }
  to   { transform: translateX(-50%); }
}

/* в”Җв”Җ INTERACTIVE ANIMATIONS в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ */

@keyframes progress-fill {
  from { width: 0%; }
  to   { width: var(--progress, 100%); }
}

@keyframes checkmark-draw {
  from { stroke-dashoffset: 100; }
  to   { stroke-dashoffset: 0; }
}

@keyframes confetti-fall {
  0%   { transform: translateY(-10px) rotate(0deg); opacity: 1; }
  100% { transform: translateY(100vh) rotate(720deg); opacity: 0; }
}

@keyframes upload-bounce {
  0%, 100% { transform: translateY(0); }
  50%       { transform: translateY(-8px); }
}

/* в”Җв”Җ DRAG ACTIVE ANIMATIONS в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ */

/* в”Җв”Җ GRADIENT TEXT ANIMATION в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ */

/* в”Җв”Җ UTILITY CLASSES в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ */

### 11.2 вҖ” GSAP Animation Implementation

```typescript
// hooks/useAnimations.ts
'use client';

import { useEffect } from 'react';
import { gsap } from 'gsap';
import { ScrollTrigger } from 'gsap/ScrollTrigger';
import { SplitText } from 'gsap/SplitText';
import { CustomEase } from 'gsap/CustomEase';

if (typeof window !== 'undefined') {
  gsap.registerPlugin(ScrollTrigger, SplitText, CustomEase);
  CustomEase.create('expo.out', 'M0,0,C0.05,0,0.133,0.166,0.166,0.25,0.196,0.328,0.224,0.5,0.5,0.8,0.63,0.896,0.786,0.99,1,1');
}

export function useToolsPageAnimations() {
  useEffect(() => {
    const ctx = gsap.context(() => {

      // в”Җв”Җ HERO HEADLINE вҖ” SplitText char-by-char в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
      const headline = document.querySelector('.hero-headline');
      if (headline) {
        const split = new SplitText(headline, { type: 'chars,words' });
        gsap.from(split.chars, {
          opacity: 0,
          y: 60,
          rotateX: -90,
          stagger: 0.015,
          duration: 0.8,
          ease: 'expo.out',
          delay: 0.2,
        });
      }

      // в”Җв”Җ HERO SUBTITLE вҖ” fade up в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
      gsap.from('.hero-subtitle', {
        opacity: 0,
        y: 30,
        duration: 0.8,
        ease: 'expo.out',
        delay: 0.5,
      });

      // в”Җв”Җ HERO STATS вҖ” staggered counters в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
      gsap.from('.hero-stat', {
        opacity: 0,
        y: 20,
        duration: 0.6,
        stagger: 0.1,
        ease: 'expo.out',
        delay: 0.7,
      });

      // в”Җв”Җ SEARCH BAR вҖ” scale in в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
      gsap.from('.hero-search', {
        opacity: 0,
        scale: 0.94,
        duration: 0.7,
        ease: 'expo.out',
        delay: 0.8,
      });

      // в”Җв”Җ FEATURED TOOL CARDS вҖ” stagger on scroll в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
      gsap.from('.featured-tool-card', {
        opacity: 0,
        y: 40,
        duration: 0.7,
        stagger: 0.08,
        ease: 'expo.out',
        scrollTrigger: {
          trigger: '.featured-tools-section',
          start: 'top 85%',
          toggleActions: 'play none none none',
        },
      });

      // в”Җв”Җ TOOL CARDS GRID вҖ” stagger reveal в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
      gsap.from('.tool-card', {
        opacity: 0,
        y: 32,
        duration: 0.5,
        stagger: { amount: 0.6, from: 'start', ease: 'none' },
        ease: 'power2.out',
        scrollTrigger: {
          trigger: '.tools-grid',
          start: 'top 80%',
          toggleActions: 'play none none none',
        },
      });

      // в”Җв”Җ STATS SECTION вҖ” number counters в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
      const statNumbers = document.querySelectorAll<HTMLElement>('[data-count]');
      statNumbers.forEach((el) => {
        const target = parseFloat(el.dataset.count || '0');
        const suffix = el.dataset.suffix || '';
        const decimals = el.dataset.decimals ? parseInt(el.dataset.decimals) : 0;

        gsap.from({ val: 0 }, {
          val: target,
          duration: 2.5,
          ease: 'power2.out',
          snap: { val: decimals === 0 ? 1 : 0.1 },
          scrollTrigger: {
            trigger: el,
            start: 'top 85%',
            once: true,
          },
          onUpdate: function() {
            const current = this.targets()[0].val;
            el.textContent = (decimals > 0 ? current.toFixed(decimals) : Math.round(current).toLocaleString()) + suffix;
          },
        });
      });

      // в”Җв”Җ HERO PARALLAX в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
      gsap.to('.hero-3d-bg', {
        y: '25%',
        ease: 'none',
        scrollTrigger: {
          trigger: '.hero-section',
          start: 'top top',
          end: 'bottom top',
          scrub: 1.5,
        },
      });

      // в”Җв”Җ SECTION HEADINGS вҖ” clip-path reveal в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
      document.querySelectorAll('.section-heading').forEach((el) => {
        gsap.from(el, {
          clipPath: 'inset(0 100% 0 0)',
          duration: 1,
          ease: 'expo.out',
          scrollTrigger: {
            trigger: el,
            start: 'top 85%',
          },
        });
      });

    });

    return () => {
      ctx.revert();
      ScrollTrigger.getAll().forEach((t) => t.kill());
    };
  }, []);
}

// в”Җв”Җ INDIVIDUAL TOOL PAGE ANIMATIONS в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
export function useToolPageAnimations() {
  useEffect(() => {
    const ctx = gsap.context(() => {

      // Upload zone floating icon
      gsap.to('.upload-icon', {
        y: -8,
        duration: 2,
        ease: 'sine.inOut',
        repeat: -1,
        yoyo: true,
      });

      // Tool hero icon 3D rotation
      gsap.to('.tool-hero-icon', {
        rotateY: 15,
        rotateX: -5,
        duration: 3,
        ease: 'sine.inOut',
        repeat: -1,
        yoyo: true,
      });

      // HOW IT WORKS вҖ” stagger
      gsap.from('.how-it-works-step', {
        opacity: 0,
        y: 30,
        duration: 0.6,
        stagger: 0.15,
        ease: 'expo.out',
        scrollTrigger: {
          trigger: '.how-it-works',
          start: 'top 80%',
        },
      });

      // Features grid
      gsap.from('.feature-item', {
        opacity: 0,
        x: -20,
        duration: 0.5,
        stagger: 0.05,
        ease: 'power2.out',
        scrollTrigger: {
          trigger: '.features-grid',
          start: 'top 85%',
        },
      });

      // Related tools
      gsap.from('.related-tool-card', {
        opacity: 0,
        x: 30,
        duration: 0.5,
        stagger: 0.06,
        ease: 'expo.out',
        scrollTrigger: {
          trigger: '.related-tools',
          start: 'top 85%',
        },
      });

    });

    return () => ctx.revert();
  }, []);
}
```

## 12. 3D EFFECTS & WEBGL SYSTEM

### 12.1 вҖ” Three.js Hero Scene

```tsx
// components/three/HeroScene.tsx
'use client';

import { Suspense, useRef, useMemo } from 'react';
import { Canvas, useFrame } from '@react-three/fiber';
import { Float, Environment, Sparkles, MeshTransmissionMaterial } from '@react-three/drei';
import { EffectComposer, Bloom, ChromaticAberration } from '@react-three/postprocessing';
import * as THREE from 'three';

// Floating 3D PDF document mesh
function PDFMesh({ position, rotation, color, delay = 0 }: {
  position: [number, number, number];
  rotation: [number, number, number];
  color: string;
  delay?: number;
}) {
  const meshRef = useRef<THREE.Mesh>(null);

  useFrame((state) => {
    if (!meshRef.current) return;
    const t = state.clock.elapsedTime + delay;
    meshRef.current.rotation.y = Math.sin(t * 0.3) * 0.15;
    meshRef.current.rotation.x = Math.sin(t * 0.2) * 0.08;
  });

  return (
    <Float speed={1.5} rotationIntensity={0.3} floatIntensity={0.6}>
      <group position={position} rotation={rotation}>
        {/* PDF page body */}
        <mesh ref={meshRef} castShadow receiveShadow>
          <boxGeometry args={[0.75, 1.05, 0.04]} />
          <MeshTransmissionMaterial
            color={color}
            transmission={0.6}
            thickness={0.05}
            roughness={0.1}
            metalness={0.2}
            opacity={0.25}
            transparent
          />
        </mesh>

        {/* PDF corner fold */}
        <mesh position={[0.275, 0.425, 0.025]}>
          <boxGeometry args={[0.2, 0.2, 0.04]} />
          <meshStandardMaterial color="#ffffff" opacity={0.1} transparent />
        </mesh>

        {/* PDF text lines */}
        {[0.3, 0.1, -0.1, -0.3].map((y, i) => (
          <mesh key={i} position={[0, y, 0.025]}>
            <boxGeometry args={[0.5, 0.02, 0.005]} />
            <meshStandardMaterial color={color} opacity={0.4} transparent />
          </mesh>
        ))}
      </group>
    </Float>
  );
}

// GPU Particle field
function ParticleField() {
  const count = 800;
  const positions = useMemo(() => {
    const pos = new Float32Array(count * 3);
    for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
      pos[i * 3]     = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 20;
      pos[i * 3 + 1] = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 15;
      pos[i * 3 + 2] = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 10 - 5;
    }
    return pos;
  }, []);

  const pointsRef = useRef<THREE.Points>(null);

  useFrame((state) => {
    if (!pointsRef.current) return;
    pointsRef.current.rotation.y = state.clock.elapsedTime * 0.02;
    pointsRef.current.rotation.x = Math.sin(state.clock.elapsedTime * 0.01) * 0.05;
  });

  return (
    <points ref={pointsRef}>
      <bufferGeometry>
        <bufferAttribute
          attach="attributes-position"
          count={count}
          array={positions}
          itemSize={3}
        />
      </bufferGeometry>
      <pointsMaterial
        size={0.025}
        color="#6366F1"
        transparent
        opacity={0.5}
        sizeAttenuation
      />
    </points>
  );
}

export function HeroScene() {
  const pdfDocuments = [
    { position: [-3.5, 1.2, -3] as [number, number, number], rotation: [0.1, 0.4, 0.1] as [number, number, number], color: '#6366F1', delay: 0 },
    { position: [3.8, -0.5, -4] as [number, number, number], rotation: [-0.1, -0.5, 0.2] as [number, number, number], color: '#8B5CF6', delay: 1 },
    { position: [-1.5, -2, -5] as [number, number, number], rotation: [0.2, 0.2, -0.1] as [number, number, number], color: '#3B82F6', delay: 2 },
    { position: [2.5, 2.5, -3] as [number, number, number], rotation: [0.15, -0.3, 0.3] as [number, number, number], color: '#10B981', delay: 0.5 },
    { position: [0.5, 0.8, -6] as [number, number, number], rotation: [0, 0.6, 0] as [number, number, number], color: '#EC4899', delay: 1.5 },
    { position: [-4, -1.5, -4] as [number, number, number], rotation: [-0.2, 0.3, 0.2] as [number, number, number], color: '#F59E0B', delay: 0.8 },
  ];

  return (
    <div className="absolute inset-0 -z-10 overflow-hidden">
      <Canvas
        camera={{ position: [0, 0, 6], fov: 70 }}
        gl={{ antialias: true, alpha: true, powerPreference: 'high-performance' }}
        dpr={[1, 2]}
      >
        <Suspense fallback={null}>
          <ambientLight intensity={0.4} />
          <directionalLight position={[5, 5, 5]} intensity={0.8} color="#6366F1" />
          <pointLight position={[-5, -5, -3]} intensity={0.4} color="#8B5CF6" />

          <ParticleField />

          {pdfDocuments.map((doc, i) => (
            <PDFMesh key={i} {...doc} />
          ))}

          <Sparkles
            count={60}
            scale={[14, 10, 10]}
            size={1.5}
            speed={0.3}
            color="#6366F1"
            opacity={0.4}
          />

          <EffectComposer>
            <Bloom
              luminanceThreshold={0.6}
              luminanceSmoothing={0.9}
              intensity={0.6}
            />
          </EffectComposer>

          <Environment preset="city" />
        </Suspense>
      </Canvas>
    </div>
  );
}

### 12.2 вҖ” Custom Cursor Follower

```tsx
// components/layout/CursorFollower.tsx
'use client';

import { useEffect, useRef } from 'react';
import { motion, useMotionValue, useSpring } from 'framer-motion';

export function CursorFollower() {
  const cursorRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
  const cursorOuterRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);

  const mouseX = useMotionValue(0);
  const mouseY = useMotionValue(0);

  const springConfig = { stiffness: 500, damping: 40 };
  const cursorX = useSpring(mouseX, springConfig);
  const cursorY = useSpring(mouseY, springConfig);

  const outerSpringConfig = { stiffness: 100, damping: 20 };
  const outerX = useSpring(mouseX, outerSpringConfig);
  const outerY = useSpring(mouseY, outerSpringConfig);

  useEffect(() => {
    const move = (e: MouseEvent) => {
      mouseX.set(e.clientX);
      mouseY.set(e.clientY);
    };

    const onHover = () => {
      cursorRef.current?.classList.add('is-hovering');
      cursorOuterRef.current?.classList.add('is-hovering');
    };
    const onLeave = () => {
      cursorRef.current?.classList.remove('is-hovering');
      cursorOuterRef.current?.classList.remove('is-hovering');
    };

    window.addEventListener('mousemove', move);

    document.querySelectorAll('a, button, [data-cursor="hover"]').forEach((el) => {
      el.addEventListener('mouseenter', onHover);
      el.addEventListener('mouseleave', onLeave);
    });

    return () => window.removeEventListener('mousemove', move);
  }, []);

  return (
    <>
      {/* Inner dot */}
      <motion.div
        ref={cursorRef}
        className="fixed top-0 left-0 w-3 h-3 bg-indigo-500 rounded-full pointer-events-none z-[9999]
                   mix-blend-difference transition-transform duration-150
                   [&.is-hovering]:scale-150 [&.is-hovering]:bg-white"
        style={{
          x: cursorX,
          y: cursorY,
          translateX: '-50%',
          translateY: '-50%',
        }}
      />

      {/* Outer ring */}
      <motion.div
        ref={cursorOuterRef}
        className="fixed top-0 left-0 w-10 h-10 border border-indigo-500/40 rounded-full
                   pointer-events-none z-[9999] mix-blend-difference
                   [&.is-hovering]:scale-200 [&.is-hovering]:border-indigo-300/60
                   transition-transform duration-300"
        style={{
          x: outerX,
          y: outerY,
          translateX: '-50%',
          translateY: '-50%',
        }}
      />
    </>
  );
}
```

### 13.1 вҖ” Main ToolCard Component (Production-Grade)

```tsx
// components/tools-listing/ToolCard.tsx
'use client';

import { useRef } from 'react';
import Link from 'next/link';
import { motion, useMotionValue, useSpring, useTransform } from 'framer-motion';
import { LucideIcon, ArrowRight, Sparkles } from 'lucide-react';
import * as LucideIcons from 'lucide-react';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
import type { Tool } from '@packages/tool-registry';

interface ToolCardProps {
  tool: Tool;
  index: number;
  variant?: 'default' | 'featured';
}

export function ToolCard({ tool, index, variant = 'default' }: ToolCardProps) {
  const cardRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);

  // Mouse parallax effect
  const mouseX = useMotionValue(0);
  const mouseY = useMotionValue(0);
  const springX = useSpring(mouseX, { stiffness: 300, damping: 30 });
  const springY = useSpring(mouseY, { stiffness: 300, damping: 30 });

  const rotateX = useTransform(springY, [-0.5, 0.5], [6, -6]);
  const rotateY = useTransform(springX, [-0.5, 0.5], [-6, 6]);
  const glareX = useTransform(springX, [-0.5, 0.5], ['0%', '100%']);
  const glareY = useTransform(springY, [-0.5, 0.5], ['0%', '100%']);

  const handleMouseMove = (e: React.MouseEvent<HTMLDivElement>) => {
    if (!cardRef.current) return;
    const rect = cardRef.current.getBoundingClientRect();
    const x = (e.clientX - rect.left) / rect.width - 0.5;
    const y = (e.clientY - rect.top) / rect.height - 0.5;
    mouseX.set(x);
    mouseY.set(y);
  };

  const handleMouseLeave = () => {
    mouseX.set(0);
    mouseY.set(0);
  };

  // Get icon component
  const IconComponent = (LucideIcons as any)[tool.icon] as LucideIcon;

  const isFeatured = variant === 'featured';

  return (
    <motion.div
      className="tool-card"
      initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 24 }}
      animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
      transition={{
        duration: 0.5,
        delay: Math.min(index * 0.04, 0.8),
        ease: [0.16, 1, 0.3, 1],
      }}
      style={{ perspective: 1000 }}
    >
      <Link href={`/tools/${tool.slug}`} tabIndex={0} aria-label={`${tool.name}: ${tool.description}`}>
        <motion.div
          ref={cardRef}
          onMouseMove={handleMouseMove}
          onMouseLeave={handleMouseLeave}
          style={{ rotateX, rotateY, transformStyle: 'preserve-3d' }}
          whileHover={{ scale: 1.02 }}
          transition={{ type: 'spring', stiffness: 400, damping: 25 }}
          className={cn(
            'group relative overflow-hidden rounded-[--radius-xl] cursor-pointer',
            'border border-[--color-border-default] bg-[--color-bg-glass]',
            'hover:border-[--color-border-strong] hover:bg-[--color-bg-glass-hover]',
            'backdrop-blur-sm',
            'transition-shadow duration-300',
            'hover:shadow-[var(--shadow-card-hover)]',
            isFeatured ? 'p-6' : 'p-4',
            // Focus styles for accessibility
            'focus-within:ring-2 focus-within:ring-indigo-500/50 focus-within:ring-offset-2 focus-within:ring-offset-[--color-bg-base]',
          )}
        >
          {/* Gradient hover background */}
          <div
            className={cn(
              'absolute inset-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100',
              'transition-opacity duration-400 rounded-[--radius-xl]',
              `bg-gradient-to-br ${tool.gradientClass}`,
            )}
          />

          {/* Glare effect */}
          <motion.div
            className="absolute inset-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity duration-300 rounded-[--radius-xl] pointer-events-none"
            style={{
              background: `radial-gradient(circle at ${glareX} ${glareY}, rgba(255,255,255,0.08) 0%, transparent 60%)`,
            }}
          />

          {/* Badges */}
          <div className="absolute top-3 right-3 flex gap-1.5 z-10">
            {tool.isNew && (
              <span className="flex items-center gap-1 text-[10px] font-bold tracking-wide
                bg-indigo-500 text-white px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full uppercase">
                <Sparkles size={8} />
                New
              </span>
            )}
            {tool.isBeta && (
              <span className="text-[10px] font-semibold
                bg-amber-500/20 text-amber-300 border border-amber-500/30
                px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full">
                Beta
              </span>
            )}
            {tool.isPremium && (
              <span className="text-[10px] font-semibold
                bg-violet-500/20 text-violet-300 border border-violet-500/30
                px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full">
                Pro
              </span>
            )}
          </div>

          {/* Icon */}
          <div
            className={cn(
              'relative z-10 rounded-2xl flex items-center justify-center mb-3',
              'transition-transform duration-200 group-hover:scale-110',
              isFeatured ? 'w-14 h-14 mb-4' : 'w-11 h-11',
            )}
            style={{ backgroundColor: `${tool.color}1A` }}
          >
            {IconComponent && (
              <IconComponent
                size={isFeatured ? 26 : 22}
                style={{ color: tool.color }}
                strokeWidth={1.5}
              />
            )}
          </div>

          {/* Content */}
          <div className="relative z-10 flex-1">
            <h3 className={cn(
              'font-semibold text-[--color-text-primary] leading-tight mb-1',
              'group-hover:text-white transition-colors duration-200',
              isFeatured ? 'text-base' : 'text-[14px]',
            )}>
              {tool.name}
            </h3>
            <p className={cn(
              'text-[--color-text-secondary] leading-relaxed',
              'group-hover:text-gray-300 transition-colors duration-200',
              isFeatured ? 'text-sm line-clamp-2' : 'text-[12px] line-clamp-2',
            )}>
              {tool.description}
            </p>
          </div>

          {/* Arrow */}
          <motion.div
            className="absolute bottom-4 right-4 text-[--color-text-muted]
              group-hover:text-white/70 transition-colors duration-200"
            initial={{ x: -4, opacity: 0 }}
            whileHover={{ x: 0, opacity: 1 }}
            animate={{ opacity: 0 }}
            whileInView={{ opacity: 0 }}
          >
            <div className="opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity duration-200">
              <ArrowRight size={14} />
            </div>
          </motion.div>

          {/* Input formats badge */}
          <div className="relative z-10 flex gap-1 mt-3 flex-wrap">
            {tool.inputFormats.slice(0, 3).map((fmt) => (
              <span
                key={fmt}
                className="text-[10px] font-medium uppercase
                  bg-white/5 border border-white/8 text-[--color-text-muted]
                  px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded"
              >
                {fmt}
              </span>
            ))}
            {tool.inputFormats.length > 3 && (
              <span className="text-[10px] text-[--color-text-muted]">
                +{tool.inputFormats.length - 3}
              </span>
            )}
            <span className="text-[10px] text-[--color-text-muted]">вҶ’</span>
            <span className="text-[10px] font-medium uppercase
              bg-white/5 border border-white/8 text-[--color-text-muted]
              px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded">
              {tool.outputFormat}
            </span>
          </div>
        </motion.div>
      </Link>
    </motion.div>
  );
}
```

### 13.2 вҖ” Smooth Scroll with Lenis + GSAP Integration

```tsx
// components/layout/SmoothScroll.tsx
'use client';

import { useEffect } from 'react';
import Lenis from '@studio-freight/lenis';
import { gsap } from 'gsap';
import { ScrollTrigger } from 'gsap/ScrollTrigger';

gsap.registerPlugin(ScrollTrigger);

export function SmoothScroll({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {
  useEffect(() => {
    const lenis = new Lenis({
      duration: 1.4,
      easing: (t: number) => Math.min(1, 1.001 - Math.pow(2, -10 * t)),
      orientation: 'vertical',
      gestureOrientation: 'vertical',
      smoothWheel: true,
      wheelMultiplier: 0.9,
      touchMultiplier: 1.8,
      infinite: false,
    });

    // Sync with GSAP for ScrollTrigger
    lenis.on('scroll', () => ScrollTrigger.update());
    gsap.ticker.add((time) => lenis.raf(time * 1000));
    gsap.ticker.lagSmoothing(0);

    // Expose globally for other components
    (window as any).__lenis = lenis;

    return () => {
      lenis.destroy();
      gsap.ticker.remove((time) => lenis.raf(time * 1000));
    };
  }, []);

  return <>{children}</>;
}
```
