## 14. BACKEND IMPLEMENTATION

### 14.1 вҖ” Fastify App Setup

```typescript
// apps/api/src/app.ts
import Fastify from 'fastify';
import { TypeBoxTypeProvider } from '@fastify/type-provider-typebox';
import cors from '@fastify/cors';
import helmet from '@fastify/helmet';
import rateLimit from '@fastify/rate-limit';
import multipart from '@fastify/multipart';
import pino from 'pino';

import { toolsRoutes } from './routes/tools.routes';
import { uploadRoutes } from './routes/upload.routes';
import { jobRoutes } from './routes/job.routes';
import { downloadRoutes } from './routes/download.routes';
import { sseRoutes } from './routes/sse.routes';

const logger = pino({
  level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
  transport: process.env.NODE_ENV === 'development'
    ? { target: 'pino-pretty', options: { colorize: true } }
    : undefined,
});

export async function buildApp() {
  const app = Fastify({
    logger,
    trustProxy: true,
    maxParamLength: 200,
  }).withTypeProvider<TypeBoxTypeProvider>();

  // в”Җв”Җв”Җ SECURITY в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  await app.register(helmet, {
    contentSecurityPolicy: {
      directives: {
        defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
        scriptSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'"],
        styleSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'"],
        imgSrc: ["'self'", 'data:', 'blob:', '*.cloudflare.com'],
        connectSrc: ["'self'", '*.ishu.fun', '*.upstash.io'],
        frameSrc: ["'none'"],
        objectSrc: ["'none'"],
      },
    },
    crossOriginEmbedderPolicy: false,
  });

  await app.register(cors, {
    origin: [
      'https://ishu.fun',
      'https://www.ishu.fun',
      ...(process.env.NODE_ENV === 'development' ? ['http://localhost:3000'] : []),
    ],
    methods: ['GET', 'POST', 'PUT', 'DELETE', 'OPTIONS'],
    credentials: true,
  });

  // в”Җв”Җв”Җ RATE LIMITING в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  await app.register(rateLimit, {
    global: true,
    max: 150,
    timeWindow: '15 minutes',
    keyGenerator: (req) => req.ip,
    errorResponseBuilder: () => ({
      error: 'Rate limit exceeded. Please wait and try again.',
      retryAfter: 60,
    }),
  });

  // в”Җв”Җв”Җ FILE UPLOAD в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  await app.register(multipart, {
    limits: {
      fileSize: 300 * 1024 * 1024,  // 300MB max
      files: 20,                      // 20 files max
      fields: 20,
    },
  });

  // в”Җв”Җв”Җ ROUTES в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  await app.register(toolsRoutes,   { prefix: '/api/tools' });
  await app.register(uploadRoutes,  { prefix: '/api/upload' });
  await app.register(jobRoutes,     { prefix: '/api/job' });
  await app.register(downloadRoutes,{ prefix: '/api/download' });
  await app.register(sseRoutes,     { prefix: '/api/sse' });

  // в”Җв”Җв”Җ HEALTH CHECK в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  app.get('/health', async () => ({
    status: 'ok',
    version: process.env.npm_package_version,
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
    uptime: process.uptime(),
  }));

  // в”Җв”Җв”Җ GLOBAL ERROR HANDLER в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  app.setErrorHandler((error, req, reply) => {
    logger.error({ err: error, url: req.url }, 'Unhandled error');

    if (error.statusCode === 429) {
      return reply.code(429).send({
        error: 'Too many requests. Please slow down.',
      });
    }

    return reply.code(error.statusCode || 500).send({
      error: process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production'
        ? 'An internal error occurred.'
        : error.message,
    });
  });

  return app;
}
```

### 14.2 вҖ” Upload Route (Complete Implementation)

```typescript
// apps/api/src/routes/upload.routes.ts
import type { FastifyInstance } from 'fastify';
import { createReadStream } from 'fs';
import { v4 as uuid } from 'uuid';
import { fromBuffer } from 'file-type';
import { r2Service } from '../services/r2.service';
import { queueService } from '../services/queue.service';
import { redis } from '../db/redis';

// Allowed MIME types (comprehensive list)
const ALLOWED_MIMES = new Set([
  'application/pdf',
  'application/msword',
  'application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.wordprocessingml.document',
  'application/vnd.ms-excel',
  'application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.spreadsheetml.sheet',
  'application/vnd.ms-powerpoint',
  'application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.presentationml.presentation',
  'image/jpeg', 'image/png', 'image/webp', 'image/gif', 'image/tiff', 'image/bmp',
  'image/heic', 'image/heif', 'image/svg+xml',
  'text/plain', 'text/html', 'text/csv', 'text/xml',
  'application/rtf',
  'application/epub+zip',
  'application/zip',
  'application/x-zip-compressed',
  'application/vnd.oasis.opendocument.text',
  'application/vnd.oasis.opendocument.spreadsheet',
]);

export async function uploadRoutes(app: FastifyInstance) {

  // Rate limit for uploads (stricter)
  app.post('/:toolSlug', {
    config: {
      rateLimit: { max: 15, timeWindow: '1 minute' },
    },
    handler: async (request, reply) => {
      const { toolSlug } = request.params as { toolSlug: string };
      const files: Express.Multer.File[] = [];
      const options: Record<string, string> = {};

      // Parse multipart
      const parts = request.parts();

      for await (const part of parts) {
        if (part.type === 'file') {
          const chunks: Buffer[] = [];

          for await (const chunk of part.file) {
            chunks.push(chunk);
          }

          const buffer = Buffer.concat(chunks);

          // в”Җв”Җ SECURITY: Real MIME type detection в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
          const detected = await fromBuffer(buffer);
          const realMime = detected?.mime || part.mimetype;

          if (!ALLOWED_MIMES.has(realMime)) {
            return reply.code(400).send({
              error: `File type '${realMime}' is not allowed.`,
              code: 'INVALID_FILE_TYPE',
            });
          }

          // в”Җв”Җ SECURITY: File size check в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
          const maxSizeMB = getMaxSize(toolSlug);
          if (buffer.length > maxSizeMB * 1024 * 1024) {
            return reply.code(413).send({
              error: `File size exceeds ${maxSizeMB}MB limit.`,
              code: 'FILE_TOO_LARGE',
            });
          }

          files.push({
            buffer,
            mimetype: realMime,
            originalname: part.filename || 'upload',
            size: buffer.length,
          } as any);

        } else if (part.type === 'field') {
          options[part.fieldname] = part.value as string;
        }
      }

      if (files.length === 0) {
        return reply.code(400).send({ error: 'No files provided.' });
      }

      // в”Җв”Җ UPLOAD TO R2 в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
      const inputKeys: string[] = [];
      const uploadId = uuid();

      for (let i = 0; i < files.length; i++) {
        const file = files[i];
        const key = `temp/${uploadId}/${i}-${file.originalname}`;

        await r2Service.upload(key, file.buffer, file.mimetype, {
          'Cache-Control': 'no-cache',
          'x-upload-id': uploadId,
        });

        inputKeys.push(key);
      }

      // в”Җв”Җ ENQUEUE JOB в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
      const job = await queueService.createJob({
        toolSlug,
        inputKeys,
        options,
        userId: (request as any).user?.id || null,
        ipHash: hashIP(request.ip),
        uploadId,
      });

      // в”Җв”Җ CACHE JOB STATUS в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
      await redis.setex(
        `job:${job.id}:status`,
        3600,
        JSON.stringify({ status: 'queued', progress: 0 })
      );

      const estimatedSec = getEstimatedTime(toolSlug, files);

      return reply.code(202).send({
        jobId: job.id,
        uploadId,
        status: 'queued',
        estimatedSeconds: estimatedSec,
        filesCount: files.length,
        totalSizeBytes: files.reduce((sum, f) => sum + f.size, 0),
      });
    },
  });
}

function getMaxSize(toolSlug: string): number {
  const sizeLimits: Record<string, number> = {
    'compress-pdf': 250,
    'merge-pdf': 150,
    'jpg-to-pdf': 200,
    'zip-to-pdf': 300,
    'cbz-to-pdf': 300,
  };
  return sizeLimits[toolSlug] || 100;
}

function getEstimatedTime(toolSlug: string, files: any[]): number {
  const heavyTools = ['ocr-pdf', 'translate-pdf', 'compress-pdf', 'chat-with-pdf', 'summarize-pdf'];
  const mediumTools = ['pdf-to-word', 'pdf-to-excel', 'pdf-to-powerpoint'];

  const totalMB = files.reduce((sum, f) => sum + f.size / (1024 * 1024), 0);
  const base = heavyTools.includes(toolSlug) ? 30 : mediumTools.includes(toolSlug) ? 15 : 6;
  return Math.ceil(base + totalMB * 0.5);
}

function hashIP(ip: string): string {
  // Simple non-reversible hash for analytics
  const { createHash } = require('crypto');
  return createHash('sha256').update(ip + process.env.IP_SALT || '').digest('hex').substring(0, 16);
}
```

### 14.3 вҖ” SSE (Server-Sent Events) for Real-Time Progress

```typescript
// apps/api/src/routes/sse.routes.ts
import type { FastifyInstance } from 'fastify';
import { Queue, QueueEvents } from 'bullmq';
import { redis } from '../db/redis';

export async function sseRoutes(app: FastifyInstance) {

  // SSE connection for job status
  app.get('/:jobId', {
    handler: async (request, reply) => {
      const { jobId } = request.params as { jobId: string };

      // Set SSE headers
      reply.raw.writeHead(200, {
        'Content-Type': 'text/event-stream',
        'Cache-Control': 'no-cache',
        'Connection': 'keep-alive',
        'X-Accel-Buffering': 'no',  // Disable Nginx buffering
        'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': 'https://ishu.fun',
      });

      // Send initial ping
      reply.raw.write(`event: connected\ndata: ${JSON.stringify({ jobId })}\n\n`);

      const queueEvents = new QueueEvents('pdf-jobs', {
        connection: redis.duplicate(),
      });

      // Listen for job events
      const sendEvent = (event: string, data: any) => {
        reply.raw.write(`event: ${event}\ndata: ${JSON.stringify(data)}\n\n`);
      };

      queueEvents.on('progress', ({ jobId: id, data }) => {
        if (id === jobId) sendEvent('progress', { progress: data });
      });

      queueEvents.on('completed', async ({ jobId: id, returnvalue }) => {
        if (id === jobId) {
          sendEvent('completed', {
            status: 'completed',
            progress: 100,
            result: returnvalue,
          });
          reply.raw.end();
          await queueEvents.close();
        }
      });

      queueEvents.on('failed', async ({ jobId: id, failedReason }) => {
        if (id === jobId) {
          sendEvent('failed', {
            status: 'failed',
            error: failedReason || 'Processing failed.',
          });
          reply.raw.end();
          await queueEvents.close();
        }
      });

      // Heartbeat every 30s to keep connection alive
      const heartbeat = setInterval(() => {
        reply.raw.write(': heartbeat\n\n');
      }, 30000);

      // Cleanup on client disconnect
      request.raw.on('close', async () => {
        clearInterval(heartbeat);
        await queueEvents.close();
      });

      // Timeout after 10 minutes
      setTimeout(async () => {
        sendEvent('timeout', { message: 'Connection timeout' });
        reply.raw.end();
        await queueEvents.close();
      }, 10 * 60 * 1000);
    },
  });
}
```

### 14.4 вҖ” Merge PDF Processor (Production-Grade)

```typescript
// apps/api/src/processors/organize/merge.processor.ts
import { PDFDocument, PDFName, PDFArray } from 'pdf-lib';
import { r2Service } from '../../services/r2.service';
import type { JobData, JobResult } from '../../types/job.types';
import { logger } from '../../lib/logger';

interface MergeOptions {
  preserve_bookmarks?: boolean;
  add_blank_page?: boolean;
  order?: number[];
}

export async function mergePDFProcessor(data: JobData): Promise<JobResult> {
  const { inputKeys, options, jobId } = data;
  const opts: MergeOptions = options as MergeOptions;

  const orderedKeys = opts.order
    ? opts.order.map((i) => inputKeys[i]).filter(Boolean)
    : inputKeys;

  logger.info({ jobId, fileCount: orderedKeys.length }, 'Starting PDF merge');

  const mergedPdf = await PDFDocument.create();
  let totalPages = 0;

  for (let i = 0; i < orderedKeys.length; i++) {
    const key = orderedKeys[i];

    // Report progress
    const progress = Math.round((i / orderedKeys.length) * 85);

    // Download from R2
    const buffer = await r2Service.download(key);

    let sourcePdf: PDFDocument;
    try {
      sourcePdf = await PDFDocument.load(buffer, {
        ignoreEncryption: true,
        throwOnInvalidObject: false,
      });
    } catch (error) {
      logger.warn({ error, key }, 'Failed to load PDF, attempting repair...');
      // Attempt repair with Ghostscript
      const repaired = await repairWithGhostscript(buffer);
      sourcePdf = await PDFDocument.load(repaired);
    }

    const pageCount = sourcePdf.getPageCount();
    const copiedPages = await mergedPdf.copyPages(
      sourcePdf,
      Array.from({ length: pageCount }, (_, i) => i)
    );

    copiedPages.forEach((page) => mergedPdf.addPage(page));

    // Add blank separator page between files
    if (opts.add_blank_page && i < orderedKeys.length - 1) {
      const lastPage = copiedPages[copiedPages.length - 1];
      const { width, height } = lastPage.getSize();
      mergedPdf.addPage([width, height]);
    }

    totalPages += pageCount;

    logger.info({ jobId, progress, file: i + 1 }, 'Merged file');
  }

  // Save with optimization
  const mergedBytes = await mergedPdf.save({
    useObjectStreams: true,  // Better compression
    addDefaultPage: false,
  });

  const outputKey = `output/${jobId}/merged-${Date.now()}.pdf`;

  await r2Service.upload(
    outputKey,
    Buffer.from(mergedBytes),
    'application/pdf',
    {
      'Content-Disposition': 'attachment; filename="merged.pdf"',
      'Cache-Control': 'no-store',
    }
  );

  // Clean up input files
  await Promise.all(inputKeys.map((key) => r2Service.delete(key).catch(() => {})));

  logger.info({ jobId, outputKey, totalPages, sizeBytes: mergedBytes.length }, 'Merge complete');

  return {
    outputKey,
    pageCount: totalPages,
    sizeBytes: mergedBytes.length,
    filename: 'merged.pdf',
    mimeType: 'application/pdf',
  };
}

async function repairWithGhostscript(buffer: Buffer): Promise<Buffer> {
  const { exec } = require('child_process');
  const { promisify } = require('util');
  const execAsync = promisify(exec);
  const tmp = require('tmp-promise');

  const inputFile = await tmp.file({ postfix: '.pdf' });
  const outputFile = await tmp.file({ postfix: '.pdf' });

  require('fs').writeFileSync(inputFile.path, buffer);

  await execAsync(
    `${process.env.GHOSTSCRIPT_PATH || 'gs'} -sDEVICE=pdfwrite -dNOPAUSE -dBATCH -dQUIET ` +
    `-sOutputFile="${outputFile.path}" "${inputFile.path}"`
  );

  return require('fs').readFileSync(outputFile.path);
}
```

## 1. PROJECT OVERVIEW

### What Is This?

The **Tools Page** for `ishu.fun` is a world-class, production-grade, fully-functional PDF & document conversion utility hub вҖ” inspired by **iLovePDF, Smallpdf, Adobe Acrobat Online, Vercel, Linear, Stripe, Notion, Apple, Figma**, and **Framer**. It offers 100+ real working tools for PDF manipulation, file conversion, image handling, and document processing.

### Core Philosophy
- **Every tool MUST work** вҖ” no placeholders, no fake UI
- **Each tool lives in its own route and folder** вҖ” clean separation
- **Speed is a feature** вҖ” lazy loading, Web Workers, streaming
- **Design is a feature** вҖ” world-class animations, 3D effects, micro-interactions
- **Mobile-first** вҖ” every pixel responsive on every screen

### Design Inspiration Board
| Website | What to steal |
|---|---|
| **Vercel** | Dark glass morphism nav, clean card grids, speed feel |
| **Linear** | Keyboard shortcuts, smooth transitions, command palette |
| **Stripe** | Gradient meshes, scroll animations, trust signals |
| **Apple** | 3D product showcases, typography, whitespace mastery |
| **Framer** | Cursor effects, hover animations, visual density |
| **Figma** | Tool category sidebar, search, icon system |
| **Notion** | Clean cards, tags, organized grid |
| **iLovePDF** | Tool cards with icons, category grouping logic |
| **Smallpdf** | Upload UX, progress bars, result download flow |
| **Adobe Acrobat** | Trust, pro feel, premium file processing UI |

---

## 2. TECH STACK вҖ” FRONTEND

### Core Framework
```
Framework:        Next.js 14 (App Router)
Language:         TypeScript 5.x
Styling:          Tailwind CSS 3.x + CSS Modules + CSS Variables
Package Manager:  pnpm (faster, disk-efficient)
```

### UI Component Libraries
```
shadcn/ui          вҖ” Headless, accessible base components
Radix UI           вҖ” Primitive accessible components (Dialog, Tabs, etc.)
Lucide React       вҖ” Modern icon set (SVG-based, tree-shakeable)
Phosphor Icons     вҖ” Rich icon variants for tools
React Icons        вҖ” Fallback icon library
Heroicons          вҖ” Tailwind-native icons
```

### Animation Libraries (ALL ACTIVE)
```
GSAP 3.x + ScrollTrigger    вҖ” Main animation engine, scroll-based reveals
                              timeline animations, stagger effects
Framer Motion 11            вҖ” React-native animations, layout animations,
                              gesture-based interactions, AnimatePresence
Three.js r165               вҖ” WebGL 3D background particles,
                              floating 3D document shapes
@react-three/fiber          вҖ” React renderer for Three.js
@react-three/drei           вҖ” Three.js helpers (OrbitControls, Float, etc.)
Lenis                       вҖ” Ultra-smooth scroll, lag-free momentum scrolling
Barba.js                    вҖ” Page transitions, SPA-like route animations
Anime.js 3.x                вҖ” SVG path animations, number counting, micro-effects
React Spring 9.x            вҖ” Physics-based spring animations
Velocity.js                 вҖ” DOM animation fallback, fast property tweening
AutoAnimate                 вҖ” Zero-config list/grid auto-animations
react-intersection-observer вҖ” Trigger animations on scroll entry
motion-number               вҖ” Animated number counters (stats)
```

### 3D & Visual Effects
```
Three.js              вҖ” 3D scene: floating PDF pages, document particles
@react-three/fiber    вҖ” JSX-based Three.js integration
@react-three/drei     вҖ” Pre-built 3D helpers
Spline (splinetool)   вҖ” Embed Spline 3D scenes (hero section background)
vanta.js              вҖ” Animated WebGL backgrounds (waves, cells, net)
tsParticles           вҖ” Configurable particle systems
react-parallax-tilt   вҖ” 3D tilt effect on tool cards
react-parallax        вҖ” Scroll-based parallax layers
```

### File Handling (Frontend)
```
react-dropzone        вҖ” Drag-and-drop file upload zone
react-pdf             вҖ” Render PDF previews in browser
pdf.js (pdfjs-dist)   вҖ” Mozilla PDF engine, render pages as canvas
file-saver            вҖ” Trigger browser file download
browser-image-compression вҖ” Client-side image compression
```

### State Management
```
Zustand 4.x           вҖ” Global state (upload queue, processing status, user prefs)
React Query (TanStack) вҖ” Server state, API caching, background refetch
Jotai                 вҖ” Atomic state for tool-level UI state
```

### Forms & Validation
```
React Hook Form 7     вҖ” High-performance forms (no re-renders)
Zod 3.x               вҖ” Schema validation (TypeScript-first)
```

### Progress & Feedback
```
react-hot-toast       вҖ” Toast notifications (upload done, error, etc.)
Sonner                вҖ” Beautiful notification stack
NProgress             вҖ” Top-bar page loading indicator
react-circular-progressbar вҖ” Circular progress for file processing
```

### Search & Filtering
```
Fuse.js               вҖ” Fuzzy search for tools (client-side, instant)
cmdk                  вҖ” Command palette (Cmd+K shortcut to search tools)
```

### Performance
```
next/image            вҖ” Automatic image optimization, lazy load
next/font             вҖ” Zero-layout-shift font loading
react-virtuoso        вҖ” Virtual list/grid for 100+ tools
@loadable/component   вҖ” Code splitting per tool route
sharp                 вҖ” Server-side image processing
web-vitals            вҖ” Monitor CWV in production
```

### Fonts (World-Class Typography)
```
Primary Display:   "Satoshi" (from Fontshare) вҖ” modern, geometric
Secondary:         "Clash Display" (from Fontshare) вҖ” strong headlines
Body:              "DM Sans" вҖ” clean, readable body text
Mono:              "JetBrains Mono" вҖ” code sections if any
```

## 3. TECH STACK вҖ” BACKEND

### Runtime & Framework
```
Runtime:    Node.js 20 LTS
Framework:  Express.js 5.x (or Fastify 4.x for speed)
Language:   TypeScript 5.x
```

### PDF Processing (Core Engines)
```
pdf-lib           вҖ” Pure JS PDF creation, merging, splitting, metadata
                    editing, page management (most tools use this)
pdf2json          вҖ” Extract text and data from PDFs
pdfjs-dist        вҖ” Server-side PDF rendering
hummus-recipe     вҖ” Advanced PDF manipulation
@pdf-lib/fontkit  вҖ” Custom font embedding in PDFs
poppler (CLI)     вҖ” System-level PDF operations via child_process
ghostscript (CLI) вҖ” High-quality PDF compression, PS conversion
libreoffice (CLI) вҖ” Word/Excel/PPT вҶ” PDF conversion (headless mode)
pandoc (CLI)      вҖ” Markdown/HTML/EPUB conversions
img2pdf           вҖ” Python script bridge for image вҶ’ PDF
pdfcpu (Go CLI)   вҖ” Ultra-fast PDF operations as microservice
```

### Image Processing
```
sharp             вҖ” Node.js image resize, compress, convert (WebP, JPEG, PNG)
jimp              вҖ” Pure JS image manipulation fallback
imagemagick (CLI) вҖ” Advanced image operations via child_process
canvas (node-canvas) вҖ” Server-side canvas rendering
```

### OCR Engine
```
tesseract.js      вҖ” Pure JS OCR engine (English + Hindi + 50+ languages)
                    Used for: OCR PDF, Scan to PDF (text extraction)
node-tesseract-ocr вҖ” Tesseract CLI wrapper (faster for large files)
```

### Document Conversion
```
libreoffice       вҖ” WordвҶ”PDF, ExcelвҶ”PDF, PPTвҶ”PDF (headless)
mammoth           вҖ” DOCX вҶ’ HTML/Markdown
xlsx              вҖ” Excel read/write (SheetJS)
officegen         вҖ” Generate DOCX, XLSX, PPTX
pptxgenjs         вҖ” Generate PowerPoint programmatically
html-pdf-node     вҖ” HTML вҶ’ PDF via puppeteer/chromium
puppeteer         вҖ” Headless Chrome for HTMLвҶ’PDF, URLвҶ’PDF
playwright        вҖ” Alternative to puppeteer
turndown          вҖ” HTML вҶ’ Markdown
marked            вҖ” Markdown вҶ’ HTML
```

### File & Archive Handling
```
archiver          вҖ” Create ZIP files
node-stream-zip   вҖ” Extract ZIP files
multer            вҖ” Multipart file upload middleware
multer-s3         вҖ” Direct upload to S3/Cloudflare R2
busboy            вҖ” Low-level file stream parser
mime-types        вҖ” File type detection
file-type         вҖ” Binary sniff file type (security)
```

### Queue & Job Processing
```
Bull / BullMQ     вҖ” Redis-backed job queue for heavy processing
                    (PDF compression, OCR can take time)
bull-board        вҖ” Admin UI for job queue monitoring
```

### File Storage
```
Cloudflare R2     вҖ” S3-compatible, zero egress fee, fast CDN
AWS S3            вҖ” Fallback/alternative
@aws-sdk/client-s3 вҖ” SDK for S3/R2 operations
multer-s3         вҖ” Stream upload direct to R2/S3
```

### Authentication (for saved files, history)
```
NextAuth.js v5    вҖ” Auth for Next.js (Google OAuth, GitHub, Email magic link)
jsonwebtoken      вҖ” JWT signing for API auth
bcryptjs          вҖ” Password hashing
```

### API Security
```
helmet            вҖ” HTTP security headers
cors              вҖ” Cross-origin config
express-rate-limit вҖ” Rate limiting (prevent abuse)
express-validator вҖ” Input validation
hpp               вҖ” HTTP parameter pollution protection
```

### Logging & Monitoring
```
winston           вҖ” Structured logging
morgan            вҖ” HTTP request logger
Sentry            вҖ” Error tracking, performance monitoring
pino              вҖ” Ultra-fast JSON logger (Fastify native)
```

---

## 4. TECH STACK вҖ” DATABASE

### Primary Database
```
PostgreSQL 16     вҖ” Main relational DB (via Supabase or Neon)
Prisma 5.x        вҖ” Type-safe ORM, migrations, Prisma Studio
```

### Cache & Sessions
```
Redis (Upstash)   вҖ” Session cache, Bull queue backend,
                    rate limit counters, temp file metadata
ioredis           вҖ” Redis client for Node.js
```

### Database Schema (Key Tables)
```sql
-- Users table
users (
  id, email, name, avatar, whatsapp_no,
  auth_provider, role, created_at, updated_at
)

-- Tool usage tracking
tool_usage (
  id, tool_slug, user_id (nullable),
  ip_hash, file_size_bytes,
  processing_time_ms, status, created_at
)

-- File processing jobs
file_jobs (
  id, job_id (bull), tool_slug, user_id,
  input_r2_key, output_r2_key,
  status, error_message, expires_at, created_at
)

-- Tools metadata (for admin to toggle tools)
tools_config (
  id, slug, name, category, description,
  is_active, is_new, is_beta,
  icon_name, sort_order, created_at
)
```

### Storage Strategy
```
Upload   вҶ’ Cloudflare R2 (temp folder, TTL 1 hour)
Process  вҶ’ Worker server (Render)
Output   вҶ’ Cloudflare R2 (output folder, TTL 24 hours)
DB       вҶ’ PostgreSQL/Supabase for metadata only
Cache    вҶ’ Redis/Upstash for job status polling
```

---

## 5. TECH STACK вҖ” DEVOPS & DEPLOYMENT

### Frontend Deployment
```
Platform:   Vercel (Pro recommended)
Domain:     ishu.fun/tools
Build:      next build (SSG + SSR hybrid)
CDN:        Vercel Edge Network (global)
Preview:    Automatic preview URLs per PR
```

### Backend Deployment
```
Platform:   Render.com (Web Service)
Runtime:    Node.js 20 Docker image
Plan:       Standard ($25/mo for always-on, no cold start)
Auto-Scale: Enabled for burst processing
```

### Queue Worker Deployment
```
Platform:   Render.com (Background Worker)
Process:    BullMQ workers for PDF jobs
Scaling:    Horizontal (add workers as load increases)
```

### Infrastructure Services
```
Database:   Supabase (PostgreSQL) вҖ” Free tier вҶ’ Pro
Cache:      Upstash Redis вҖ” Serverless, pay-per-use
Storage:    Cloudflare R2 вҖ” Zero egress, S3-compatible
Monitoring: Sentry (error tracking)
Analytics:  Vercel Analytics + PostHog
CI/CD:      GitHub Actions
```

### CI/CD Pipeline (GitHub Actions)
```yaml
Triggers: Push to main, PR to main
Steps:
  1. Type check (tsc --noEmit)
  2. Lint (ESLint + Prettier)
  3. Unit tests (Vitest)
  4. Build (next build)
  5. Deploy to Vercel (frontend)
  6. Deploy to Render (backend) via webhook
```

в”Ӯ       в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ       в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ рҹ“Ғ services/
в”Ӯ       в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ r2.service.ts        # Cloudflare R2 operations
в”Ӯ       в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ queue.service.ts     # BullMQ job creation
в”Ӯ       в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ cache.service.ts     # Redis caching
в”Ӯ       в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ ai.service.ts        # OpenAI/Claude API for AI tools
в”Ӯ       в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ       в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ рҹ“Ғ db/
в”Ӯ       в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ prisma.ts            # Prisma client singleton
в”Ӯ       в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ рҹ“Ғ migrations/
в”Ӯ       в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ       в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ рҹ“Ғ config/

в”Ӯ       в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ

в”Ӯ       в”Ӯ

в”Ӯ       в”ңв”Җв”Җ Dockerfile

в”Ӯ
в”ңв”Җв”Җ рҹ“Ғ packages/                         # Shared utilities (monorepo)
в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ рҹ“Ғ shared-types/                 # Shared TypeScript types
в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ рҹ“Ғ tool-registry/               # Master list of all tools (shared)
в”Ӯ
в”ңв”Җв”Җ рҹ“Ғ docs/
в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ TOOLS.MD                         # This file
в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ API.MD                           # API documentation
в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ DEPLOYMENT.MD                   # Deployment guide
в”Ӯ
в”ңв”Җв”Җ .github/

в””в”Җв”Җ package.json

## 7. TOOLS INVENTORY (ALL 100+ TOOLS)

### Complete Master Registry

```typescript
// lib/tools-config.ts
// This is the single source of truth for all tools

export type ToolCategory =
  | 'organize'
  | 'convert-from-pdf'
  | 'convert-to-pdf'
  | 'image-tools'
  | 'pdf-security'
  | 'edit-tools'
  | 'ai-tools'
  | 'extract-tools'
  | 'advanced';

export interface Tool {
  slug: string;
  name: string;
  description: string;
  category: ToolCategory;
  icon: string;          // Phosphor icon name or Lucide icon name
  color: string;         // Accent color for card
  gradient: string;      // CSS gradient for card background
  inputFormats: string[];
  outputFormat: string;
  maxFileSizeMB: number;
  isNew?: boolean;
  isBeta?: boolean;
  isPremium?: boolean;
  backendProcessor: string; // processor filename
  relatedTools: string[];   // slugs
}

## 8. PAGE-BY-PAGE DESIGN BLUEPRINT

### 8.1 вҖ” Main Tools Listing Page (`/tools`)

#### Layout Sections (top to bottom):

```

## 9. FRONTEND IMPLEMENTATION GUIDE

### 9.1 вҖ” ToolCard Component

```tsx
// components/tools-page/ToolCard.tsx
'use client';

import { motion } from 'framer-motion';
import { useRouter } from 'next/navigation';
import Link from 'next/link';
import { Tool } from '@/lib/tools-config';
import * as PhosphorIcons from 'phosphor-react';

interface ToolCardProps {
  tool: Tool;
  index: number;
}

export function ToolCard({ tool, index }: ToolCardProps) {
  const IconComponent = (PhosphorIcons as any)[tool.icon];

  return (
    <motion.div
      initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 20 }}
      animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
      transition={{
        duration: 0.4,
        delay: index * 0.05,
        ease: [0.25, 0.46, 0.45, 0.94]
      }}
      whileHover={{
        y: -4,
        transition: { duration: 0.2 }
      }}
      className="group relative"
    >
      <Link href={`/tools/${tool.slug}`}>
        <div
          className={`
            relative overflow-hidden rounded-[20px] p-5 cursor-pointer
            border border-white/8 bg-white/[0.03]
            hover:border-white/15 hover:bg-white/[0.06]
            transition-all duration-300
            backdrop-blur-sm
          `}
        >
          {/* Gradient background on hover */}
          <div
            className={`
              absolute inset-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100
              transition-opacity duration-300 rounded-[20px]
              bg-gradient-to-br ${tool.gradient}
            `}
          />

          {/* New badge */}
          {tool.isNew && (
            <span className="absolute top-3 right-3 text-[10px] font-semibold
              bg-blue-500 text-white px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full z-10">
              NEW
            </span>
          )}

          {/* Icon */}
          <div
            className="relative z-10 w-12 h-12 rounded-2xl flex items-center
              justify-center mb-4"
            style={{ backgroundColor: `${tool.color}20` }}
          >
            {IconComponent && (
              <IconComponent
                size={24}
                weight="duotone"
                style={{ color: tool.color }}
              />
            )}
          </div>

          {/* Content */}
          <div className="relative z-10">
            <h3 className="font-semibold text-white text-[15px] mb-1 group-hover:text-white
              transition-colors duration-200">
              {tool.name}
            </h3>
            <p className="text-gray-400 text-[13px] leading-relaxed line-clamp-2
              group-hover:text-gray-300 transition-colors duration-200">
              {tool.description}
            </p>
          </div>

          {/* Arrow on hover */}
          <motion.div
            className="absolute bottom-4 right-4 text-white/0 group-hover:text-white/60
              transition-colors duration-200"
            initial={{ x: -4, opacity: 0 }}
            whileHover={{ x: 0, opacity: 1 }}
          >
            вҶ’
          </motion.div>
        </div>
      </Link>
    </motion.div>
  );
}
```

### 9.2 вҖ” File Upload Zone Component

```tsx
// components/tool-page/FileUploadZone.tsx
'use client';

import { useCallback, useState } from 'react';
import { useDropzone } from 'react-dropzone';
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion';
import { CloudArrowUp, File, X } from 'phosphor-react';
import { toast } from 'sonner';

interface FileUploadZoneProps {
  acceptedFormats: string[];
  maxSizeMB: number;
  multiple?: boolean;
  onFilesAccepted: (files: File[]) => void;
}

export function FileUploadZone({
  acceptedFormats,
  maxSizeMB,
  multiple = false,
  onFilesAccepted,
}: FileUploadZoneProps) {
  const [uploadedFiles, setUploadedFiles] = useState<File[]>([]);

  const onDrop = useCallback((acceptedFiles: File[], rejectedFiles: any[]) => {
    if (rejectedFiles.length > 0) {
      toast.error('Some files were rejected. Check format and size limits.');
      return;
    }
    setUploadedFiles(acceptedFiles);
    onFilesAccepted(acceptedFiles);
  }, [onFilesAccepted]);

  const { getRootProps, getInputProps, isDragActive, isDragReject } = useDropzone({
    onDrop,
    accept: acceptedFormats.reduce((acc, fmt) => {
      acc[`application/${fmt}`] = [`.${fmt}`];
      return acc;
    }, {} as Record<string, string[]>),
    maxSize: maxSizeMB * 1024 * 1024,
    multiple,
  });

  return (
    <div className="w-full">
      <motion.div
        {...getRootProps()}
        animate={{
          borderColor: isDragActive
            ? isDragReject ? '#EF4444' : '#3B82F6'
            : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)',
          backgroundColor: isDragActive
            ? 'rgba(59,130,246,0.05)'
            : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.02)',
        }}
        transition={{ duration: 0.2 }}
        className={`
          relative min-h-[240px] rounded-2xl border-2 border-dashed
          flex flex-col items-center justify-center cursor-pointer
          transition-all duration-200 group p-8
        `}
      >
        <input {...getInputProps()} />

        {/* Animated background pulse */}
        {isDragActive && (
          <motion.div
            className="absolute inset-0 rounded-2xl bg-blue-500/5"
            animate={{ scale: [1, 1.02, 1] }}
            transition={{ duration: 0.5, repeat: Infinity }}
          />
        )}

        <motion.div
          animate={{ y: isDragActive ? -8 : 0 }}
          transition={{ duration: 0.3 }}
          className="flex flex-col items-center gap-3 text-center relative z-10"
        >
          <div className="w-16 h-16 rounded-2xl bg-blue-500/10 flex items-center
            justify-center group-hover:bg-blue-500/20 transition-colors duration-200">
            <CloudArrowUp size={32} className="text-blue-400" weight="duotone" />
          </div>

          <div>
            <p className="text-white font-semibold text-lg mb-1">
              {isDragActive ? 'Drop your files here' : 'Upload your file'}
            </p>
            <p className="text-gray-400 text-sm">
              Drag & drop or{' '}
              <span className="text-blue-400 hover:underline">browse files</span>
            </p>
          </div>

          <div className="flex gap-2 flex-wrap justify-center mt-2">
            {acceptedFormats.map(fmt => (
              <span key={fmt}
                className="text-xs bg-white/5 border border-white/10
                  text-gray-400 px-2 py-1 rounded-md uppercase">
                {fmt}
              </span>
            ))}
            <span className="text-xs bg-white/5 border border-white/10
              text-gray-400 px-2 py-1 rounded-md">
              Max {maxSizeMB}MB
            </span>
          </div>
        </motion.div>
      </motion.div>

      {/* Uploaded files list */}
      <AnimatePresence>
        {uploadedFiles.length > 0 && (
          <motion.div
            initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 10 }}
            animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
            exit={{ opacity: 0, y: 10 }}
            className="mt-4 space-y-2"
          >
            {uploadedFiles.map((file, i) => (
              <motion.div
                key={i}
                initial={{ opacity: 0, x: -10 }}
                animate={{ opacity: 1, x: 0 }}
                transition={{ delay: i * 0.05 }}
                className="flex items-center gap-3 bg-white/[0.03] border
                  border-white/8 rounded-xl p-3"
              >
                <File size={20} className="text-blue-400 shrink-0" weight="duotone" />
                <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                  <p className="text-white text-sm font-medium truncate">{file.name}</p>
                  <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs">
                    {(file.size / 1024 / 1024).toFixed(2)} MB
                  </p>
                </div>
                <button
                  onClick={(e) => {
                    e.stopPropagation();
                    setUploadedFiles(prev => prev.filter((_, idx) => idx !== i));
                  }}
                  className="text-gray-500 hover:text-red-400 transition-colors p-1 rounded"
                >
                  <X size={16} />
                </button>
              </motion.div>
            ))}
          </motion.div>
        )}
      </AnimatePresence>
    </div>
  );
}
```

### 9.3 вҖ” GSAP Scroll Animations Setup

```tsx
// hooks/useAnimations.ts
'use client';

import { useEffect } from 'react';
import { gsap } from 'gsap';
import { ScrollTrigger } from 'gsap/ScrollTrigger';

gsap.registerPlugin(ScrollTrigger);

export function useToolsPageAnimations() {
  useEffect(() => {
    // Stagger animate tool cards on scroll
    const cards = document.querySelectorAll('.tool-card');
    gsap.fromTo(cards, 
      { opacity: 0, y: 30 },
      {
        opacity: 1,
        y: 0,
        duration: 0.5,
        stagger: 0.04,
        ease: 'power2.out',
        scrollTrigger: {
          trigger: '.tools-grid',
          start: 'top 80%',
          toggleActions: 'play none none none',
        }
      }
    );

    // Stats counter animation
    const stats = document.querySelectorAll('.stat-number');
    stats.forEach((stat) => {
      const target = parseInt(stat.getAttribute('data-target') || '0');
      gsap.fromTo(
        { value: 0 },
        {
          value: target,
          duration: 2,
          ease: 'power1.out',
          scrollTrigger: {
            trigger: stat,
            start: 'top 85%',
            once: true,
          },
          onUpdate: function() {
            stat.textContent = Math.round(this.targets()[0].value).toLocaleString();
          }
        }
      );
    });

    // Hero parallax
    gsap.to('.hero-bg', {
      y: '30%',
      ease: 'none',
      scrollTrigger: {
        trigger: '.hero-section',
        start: 'top top',
        end: 'bottom top',
        scrub: 1,
      }
    });

    return () => {
      ScrollTrigger.getAll().forEach(t => t.kill());
    };
  }, []);
}
```

### 9.4 вҖ” Smooth Scroll Setup (Lenis)

```tsx
// components/shared/SmoothScroll.tsx
'use client';

import { useEffect } from 'react';
import Lenis from '@studio-freight/lenis';
import { gsap } from 'gsap';
import { ScrollTrigger } from 'gsap/ScrollTrigger';

export function SmoothScroll({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {
  useEffect(() => {
    const lenis = new Lenis({
      duration: 1.2,
      easing: (t) => Math.min(1, 1.001 - Math.pow(2, -10 * t)),
      orientation: 'vertical',
      gestureOrientation: 'vertical',
      smoothWheel: true,
      wheelMultiplier: 1,
      touchMultiplier: 2,
    });

    // Sync Lenis with GSAP ScrollTrigger
    lenis.on('scroll', ScrollTrigger.update);
    gsap.ticker.add((time) => lenis.raf(time * 1000));
    gsap.ticker.lagSmoothing(0);

    return () => {
      lenis.destroy();
    };
  }, []);

  return <>{children}</>;
}
```

### 9.5 вҖ” Three.js Floating Documents Background

```tsx
// components/three/FloatingDocuments.tsx
'use client';

import { Canvas, useFrame } from '@react-three/fiber';
import { Float, MeshDistortMaterial } from '@react-three/drei';
import { useRef } from 'react';
import * as THREE from 'three';

function FloatingDoc({ position, rotation, color }: any) {
  const meshRef = useRef<THREE.Mesh>(null);

  useFrame((state) => {
    if (meshRef.current) {
      meshRef.current.rotation.y = Math.sin(state.clock.elapsedTime * 0.3) * 0.2;
    }
  });

  return (
    <Float speed={2} rotationIntensity={0.5} floatIntensity={0.5}>
      <mesh ref={meshRef} position={position} rotation={rotation} castShadow>
        <boxGeometry args={[0.8, 1.1, 0.05]} />
        <meshStandardMaterial
          color={color}
          transparent
          opacity={0.15}
          wireframe={false}
          roughness={0.2}
          metalness={0.8}
        />
      </mesh>
    </Float>
  );
}

export function FloatingDocuments() {
  const docs = [
    { position: [-3, 1, -2], rotation: [0.1, 0.3, 0.1], color: '#3B82F6' },
    { position: [3, -1, -3], rotation: [-0.1, -0.4, 0.2], color: '#8B5CF6' },
    { position: [-1, -2, -4], rotation: [0.2, 0.1, -0.1], color: '#10B981' },
    { position: [2, 2, -2], rotation: [0.15, -0.2, 0.3], color: '#F59E0B' },
    { position: [0, 0, -5], rotation: [0, 0.5, 0], color: '#EF4444' },
  ];

  return (
    <div className="absolute inset-0 -z-10">
      <Canvas
        camera={{ position: [0, 0, 5], fov: 75 }}
        gl={{ antialias: true, alpha: true }}
      >
        <ambientLight intensity={0.5} />
        <pointLight position={[10, 10, 10]} intensity={0.8} />
        {docs.map((doc, i) => (
          <FloatingDoc key={i} {...doc} />
        ))}
      </Canvas>
    </div>
  );
}
```

### 9.6 вҖ” Command Palette (Cmd+K Search)

```tsx
// components/tools-page/CommandPalette.tsx
'use client';

import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { Command } from 'cmdk';
import { TOOLS } from '@/lib/tools-config';
import { useRouter } from 'next/navigation';
import Fuse from 'fuse.js';

const fuse = new Fuse(TOOLS, {
  keys: ['name', 'description', 'category'],
  threshold: 0.4,
});

export function CommandPalette() {
  const [open, setOpen] = useState(false);
  const [query, setQuery] = useState('');
  const router = useRouter();

  // Toggle with Cmd+K / Ctrl+K
  useEffect(() => {
    const down = (e: KeyboardEvent) => {
      if (e.key === 'k' && (e.metaKey || e.ctrlKey)) {
        e.preventDefault();
        setOpen(prev => !prev);
      }
    };
    document.addEventListener('keydown', down);
    return () => document.removeEventListener('keydown', down);
  }, []);

  const results = query
    ? fuse.search(query).map(r => r.item)
    : TOOLS.slice(0, 8);

  return (
    <>
      {/* Trigger button */}
      <button
        onClick={() => setOpen(true)}
        className="flex items-center gap-2 bg-white/5 border border-white/10
          rounded-xl px-4 py-2.5 text-gray-400 text-sm hover:bg-white/8
          hover:border-white/15 transition-all duration-200"
      >
        <span>Search 100+ tools...</span>
        <kbd className="text-[10px] bg-white/10 rounded px-1.5 py-0.5 ml-auto">вҢҳK</kbd>
      </button>

      {/* Palette modal */}
      {open && (
        <div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 flex items-start justify-center pt-[15vh]">
          <div
            className="fixed inset-0 bg-black/60 backdrop-blur-sm"
            onClick={() => setOpen(false)}
          />
          <Command
            className="relative z-50 w-full max-w-xl bg-[#111116] border
              border-white/10 rounded-2xl shadow-2xl overflow-hidden"
          >
            <Command.Input
              value={query}
              onValueChange={setQuery}
              placeholder="Search tools..."
              className="w-full bg-transparent px-4 py-4 text-white placeholder-gray-500
                border-b border-white/8 outline-none text-sm"
            />
            <Command.List className="max-h-80 overflow-y-auto py-2">
              {results.map(tool => (
                <Command.Item
                  key={tool.slug}
                  onSelect={() => {
                    router.push(`/tools/${tool.slug}`);
                    setOpen(false);
                  }}
                  className="flex items-center gap-3 px-4 py-3 cursor-pointer
                    hover:bg-white/5 transition-colors duration-100 rounded-lg mx-2"
                >
                  <span className="text-sm text-white font-medium">{tool.name}</span>
                  <span className="text-xs text-gray-500 ml-auto">{tool.category}</span>
                </Command.Item>
              ))}
            </Command.List>
          </Command>
        </div>
      )}
    </>
  );
}
```

## 10. BACKEND IMPLEMENTATION GUIDE

### 10.1 вҖ” Express App Setup

```typescript
// apps/api/src/app.ts
import express from 'express';
import cors from 'cors';
import helmet from 'helmet';
import { rateLimit } from 'express-rate-limit';
import morgan from 'morgan';
import { toolsRouter } from './routes/tools.routes';
import { uploadRouter } from './routes/upload.routes';
import { jobRouter } from './routes/job.routes';
import { downloadRouter } from './routes/download.routes';

const app = express();

// Security
app.use(helmet());
app.use(cors({
  origin: process.env.FRONTEND_URL || 'https://ishu.fun',
  credentials: true,
}));

// Rate limiting
const limiter = rateLimit({
  windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutes
  max: 100, // 100 requests per window
  message: { error: 'Too many requests, please try again later.' },
  standardHeaders: true,
  legacyHeaders: false,
});
app.use('/api', limiter);

// Stricter limit for heavy operations
const uploadLimiter = rateLimit({
  windowMs: 60 * 1000, // 1 minute
  max: 10, // 10 uploads per minute
});
app.use('/api/upload', uploadLimiter);

// Body parsing
app.use(express.json({ limit: '10mb' }));
app.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true }));
app.use(morgan('combined'));

// Routes
app.use('/api/tools', toolsRouter);
app.use('/api/upload', uploadRouter);
app.use('/api/job', jobRouter);
app.use('/api/download', downloadRouter);

// Health check
app.get('/health', (req, res) => {
  res.json({ status: 'ok', timestamp: new Date().toISOString() });
});

export default app;
```

### 10.2 вҖ” Upload Route

```typescript
// apps/api/src/routes/upload.routes.ts
import { Router } from 'express';
import multer from 'multer';
import { S3Client, PutObjectCommand } from '@aws-sdk/client-s3';
import { v4 as uuid } from 'uuid';
import { queueService } from '../services/queue.service';
import { r2Service } from '../services/r2.service';
import mime from 'mime-types';

const router = Router();

// In-memory storage for temp processing
const upload = multer({
  storage: multer.memoryStorage(),
  limits: { fileSize: 200 * 1024 * 1024 }, // 200MB max
  fileFilter: (req, file, cb) => {
    // Security: validate MIME type via file-type
    const allowed = ['application/pdf', 'image/jpeg', 'image/png',
      'image/webp', 'image/gif', 'application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.wordprocessingml.document',
      'application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.spreadsheetml.sheet',
      // ... all allowed types
    ];
    cb(null, true); // Additional validation in controller
  },
});

router.post('/:toolSlug', upload.array('files', 20), async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const { toolSlug } = req.params;
    const files = req.files as Express.Multer.File[];
    const options = req.body; // Tool-specific options

    if (!files || files.length === 0) {
      return res.status(400).json({ error: 'No files provided' });
    }

    // Upload files to R2 (temp bucket)
    const inputKeys: string[] = [];
    for (const file of files) {
      const key = `temp/${uuid()}-${file.originalname}`;
      await r2Service.upload(key, file.buffer, file.mimetype);
      inputKeys.push(key);
    }

    // Create job in queue
    const job = await queueService.createJob({
      toolSlug,
      inputKeys,
      options,
      userId: (req as any).user?.id,
    });

    res.json({
      jobId: job.id,
      status: 'queued',
      estimatedTime: getEstimatedTime(toolSlug, files),
    });

  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Upload error:', error);
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Upload failed. Please try again.' });
  }
});

function getEstimatedTime(toolSlug: string, files: Express.Multer.File[]): number {
  const heavyTools = ['ocr-pdf', 'translate-pdf', 'compress-pdf'];
  const base = heavyTools.includes(toolSlug) ? 30 : 10;
  const sizeMultiplier = files.reduce((sum, f) => sum + f.size, 0) / (1024 * 1024 * 10);
  return Math.ceil(base + sizeMultiplier);
}

export { router as uploadRouter };
```

### 10.3 вҖ” Merge PDF Processor

```typescript
// apps/api/src/processors/pdf/merge.processor.ts
import { PDFDocument } from 'pdf-lib';
import { r2Service } from '../../services/r2.service';

export async function mergePDFProcessor(
  inputKeys: string[],
  options: { order?: number[] }
) {
  // Sort by order if provided
  const orderedKeys = options.order
    ? options.order.map(i => inputKeys[i])
    : inputKeys;

  // Create new PDF
  const mergedPdf = await PDFDocument.create();

  for (const key of orderedKeys) {
    // Download from R2
    const buffer = await r2Service.download(key);
    const pdf = await PDFDocument.load(buffer);

    // Copy all pages
    const copiedPages = await mergedPdf.copyPages(pdf, pdf.getPageIndices());
    copiedPages.forEach(page => mergedPdf.addPage(page));
  }

  // Save merged PDF
  const mergedBytes = await mergedPdf.save();
  const outputKey = `output/${Date.now()}-merged.pdf`;
  await r2Service.upload(outputKey, Buffer.from(mergedBytes), 'application/pdf');

  return {
    outputKey,
    pageCount: mergedPdf.getPageCount(),
    sizeBytes: mergedBytes.length,
  };
}
```

### 10.4 вҖ” Job Status Polling

```typescript
// apps/api/src/routes/job.routes.ts
import { Router } from 'express';
import { Queue } from 'bullmq';
import { redis } from '../db/redis';

const router = Router();
const pdfQueue = new Queue('pdf-jobs', { connection: redis });

router.get('/:jobId', async (req, res) => {
  const { jobId } = req.params;

  const job = await pdfQueue.getJob(jobId);
  if (!job) {
    return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Job not found' });
  }

  const state = await job.getState();
  const progress = job.progress as number;

  if (state === 'completed') {
    const result = job.returnvalue;
    // Generate presigned download URL
    const downloadUrl = await r2Service.getPresignedUrl(result.outputKey, 3600);

    return res.json({
      status: 'completed',
      progress: 100,
      downloadUrl,
      metadata: {
        pageCount: result.pageCount,
        sizeBytes: result.sizeBytes,
        processedAt: job.finishedOn,
      }
    });
  }

  if (state === 'failed') {
    return res.json({
      status: 'failed',
      progress: 0,
      error: job.failedReason || 'Processing failed. Please try again.',
    });
  }

  res.json({
    status: state,
    progress: progress || 0,
  });
});

export { router as jobRouter };
```

## 11. API ROUTES & ENDPOINTS

### Complete API Reference

```
BASE URL: https://api.ishu.fun

# Tool Operations
POST   /api/upload/:toolSlug          Upload file(s) and start processing
GET    /api/job/:jobId                Get job status (poll this every 1-2s)
GET    /api/download/:outputKey       Download result (with auth token)
DELETE /api/job/:jobId                Cancel a job

# Tools Metadata
GET    /api/tools                     List all tools with metadata
GET    /api/tools/:slug               Get single tool details

# User (optional auth)
POST   /api/auth/register             Register with email/whatsapp
POST   /api/auth/login                Login
GET    /api/user/history              Get user's file history
DELETE /api/user/history/:jobId       Delete from history

# Admin
GET    /api/admin/stats               Usage statistics
PUT    /api/admin/tools/:slug         Update tool config (enable/disable)
GET    /api/admin/jobs                List all jobs (paginated)

# Health
GET    /health                        Service health check
```

## 12. ANIMATION & 3D EFFECTS SYSTEM

### Animation Playbook

```
Page Load:
  1. Navbar fades in (0.3s)
  2. Hero headline reveals via clip-path (0.6s delay 0.3s)
  3. Hero subtext fades up (0.4s delay 0.5s)
  4. Search bar scales in from 0.95 (0.4s delay 0.6s)
  5. Stats counter starts from 0 (1.5s)
  6. Category tabs slide in from left, staggered 0.05s each
  7. Tool cards fade+slide up, staggered 0.04s each (on scroll)

Scroll:
  - Category nav becomes sticky + gets glassmorphism
  - Cards have parallax shift (mouse-follow tilt via react-parallax-tilt)
  - Stats section: numbers animate to final value
  - Section headers: clip-path reveal on scroll entry

Hover States:
  - Tool cards: lift up 4px, border brightens, gradient appears
  - CTA buttons: subtle scale (1.02), glow ring
  - Nav links: underline slide animation

Tool Page Transitions (Barba.js):
  - Exit: page fades out + slides left (300ms)
  - Enter: new page fades in + slides from right (300ms)
  - During: loading bar at top

Upload Zone:
  - Idle: dashed border, subtle float animation on icon
  - Drag over: border glows blue, background lightens, icon bounces
  - Files dropped: smooth list reveal with spring physics
  - Processing: animated gradient progress bar + rotating icon
  - Complete: green checkmark with confetti burst
```

### Performance Checklist

```
Core Web Vitals Targets:
  LCP (Largest Contentful Paint): < 1.5s
  FID (First Input Delay):        < 50ms
  CLS (Cumulative Layout Shift):  < 0.05

Implementation:
  вң… next/image for all images (auto WebP, lazy load)
  вң… next/font (zero-FOUT font loading)
  вң… Dynamic imports for heavy Three.js components
  вң… Virtual scrolling (react-virtuoso) for tools grid
  вң… Route-level code splitting (Next.js automatic)
  вң… Preload critical CSS, defer non-critical
  вң… Service Worker for offline tool pages
  вң… Cloudflare CDN for R2 file delivery
  вң… Brotli compression on API server
  вң… Redis caching for /api/tools response (TTL 5min)
  вң… Incremental Static Regeneration for tool pages
  вң… Skeleton loading states (no layout shift)
```

## 14. SECURITY IMPLEMENTATION

```
File Upload Security:
  вң… Validate file MIME type using 'file-type' (binary sniffing)
  вң… Reject files with mismatched extension vs MIME
  вң… Virus scanning via ClamAV (optional, async)
  вң… Files auto-deleted from R2 after 24 hours (TTL)
  вң… No files stored permanently without user account

API Security:
  вң… Rate limiting per IP (express-rate-limit)
  вң… Helmet.js for security headers
  вң… CORS restricted to ishu.fun domain
  вң… Input validation (Zod schemas on all inputs)
  вң… No SQL injection risk (Prisma ORM)
  вң… JWT tokens for optional auth

Privacy:
  вң… Files processed in isolated temp containers
  вң… No file content logged (only metadata)
  вң… GDPR-compliant data handling
  вң… Clear data deletion policy
```

---

## 15. DEPLOYMENT GUIDE (VERCEL + RENDER)

### Frontend: Deploy to Vercel

```bash
# 1. Install Vercel CLI
npm i -g vercel

# 2. Login
vercel login

# 3. Deploy from web/ directory
cd apps/web
vercel

# 4. Set environment variables in Vercel Dashboard:
#    NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL=https://api.ishu.fun
#    NEXT_PUBLIC_APP_URL=https://ishu.fun

# 5. Add custom domain in Vercel Dashboard
#    Domain: ishu.fun
#    Route /tools/* to this deployment

# vercel.json
{
  "rewrites": [
    { "source": "/tools/(.*)", "destination": "/tools/$1" }
  ],
  "headers": [
    {
      "source": "/(.*)",
      "headers": [
        { "key": "X-Content-Type-Options", "value": "nosniff" },
        { "key": "X-Frame-Options", "value": "DENY" },
        { "key": "X-XSS-Protection", "value": "1; mode=block" }
      ]
    }
  ]
}
```

### Backend: Deploy to Render

```yaml
# render.yaml (in apps/api/)

services:
  # Main API service
  - type: web
    name: ishu-tools-api
    env: node
    plan: standard
    buildCommand: pnpm install && pnpm build
    startCommand: pnpm start
    envVars:
      - key: DATABASE_URL
        fromDatabase:
          name: ishu-db
          property: connectionString
      - key: REDIS_URL
        sync: false
      - key: R2_ACCOUNT_ID
        sync: false
      - key: R2_ACCESS_KEY_ID
        sync: false
      - key: R2_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY
        sync: false
      - key: R2_BUCKET_NAME
        sync: false
      - key: FRONTEND_URL
        value: https://ishu.fun
      - key: NODE_ENV
        value: production

  # BullMQ Worker (separate process)
  - type: worker
    name: ishu-tools-worker
    env: node
    plan: standard
    buildCommand: pnpm install && pnpm build
    startCommand: node dist/workers/pdf.worker.js
    envVars:
      - key: DATABASE_URL
        fromDatabase:
          name: ishu-db
          property: connectionString
      - key: REDIS_URL
        sync: false

databases:
  - name: ishu-db
    databaseName: ishu_tools
    user: ishu_admin
    plan: starter
```

## 16. ENVIRONMENT VARIABLES

```env
# apps/web/.env.local (Frontend)
NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL=https://api.ishu.fun
NEXT_PUBLIC_APP_URL=https://ishu.fun
NEXT_PUBLIC_R2_PUBLIC_URL=https://files.ishu.fun

# apps/api/.env (Backend)
# Server
PORT=3001
NODE_ENV=production
FRONTEND_URL=https://ishu.fun

# Database
DATABASE_URL=postgresql://user:password@host:5432/ishu_tools

# Redis (Upstash)
REDIS_URL=rediss://default:token@region.upstash.io:6379

# Cloudflare R2
R2_ACCOUNT_ID=your_cloudflare_account_id
R2_ACCESS_KEY_ID=your_r2_access_key
R2_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY=your_r2_secret_key
R2_BUCKET_NAME=ishu-tools-files
R2_PUBLIC_URL=https://files.ishu.fun

# Auth (NextAuth)
NEXTAUTH_SECRET=your_random_32_char_secret
NEXTAUTH_URL=https://ishu.fun
GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID=your_google_oauth_id
GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET=your_google_oauth_secret

# AI Services (for AI tools)
OPENAI_API_KEY=sk-...
ANTHROPIC_API_KEY=sk-ant-...

# Sentry
SENTRY_DSN=https://...

# LibreOffice (path on server)
LIBREOFFICE_PATH=/usr/bin/libreoffice
GHOSTSCRIPT_PATH=/usr/bin/gs
TESSERACT_PATH=/usr/bin/tesseract
```

## 17. TESTING STRATEGY

```
Unit Tests (Vitest):
  - Each processor function (merge, split, compress...)
  - Utility functions (file type validation, size formatting)
  - React components (ToolCard, FileUploadZone)
  - Target: 80% coverage on processors

Integration Tests:
  - API endpoint tests (supertest)
  - Upload вҶ’ process вҶ’ download full flow
  - Queue job creation and completion

E2E Tests (Playwright):
  - User uploads PDF вҶ’ merges вҶ’ downloads
  - Search tools functionality
  - Command palette (Cmd+K)
  - Mobile upload flow

Performance Tests:
  - Lighthouse CI (target score: 95+)
  - Load test 100 concurrent uploads
  - Core Web Vitals monitoring

Run tests:
  pnpm test          # Unit tests
  pnpm test:e2e      # Playwright E2E
  pnpm test:perf     # Performance
```

## 18. ACCESSIBILITY (A11Y)

```
Standards: WCAG 2.1 AA

Implementations:
  вң… Semantic HTML5 elements (main, nav, section, article)
  вң… ARIA labels on all icon-only buttons
  вң… Keyboard navigation for all interactive elements
  вң… Focus visible styles (visible focus rings)
  вң… Color contrast ratio вүҘ 4.5:1 for all text
  вң… Alt text on all images
  вң… Skip-to-content link
  вң… Reduced motion support:
       @media (prefers-reduced-motion: reduce) {
         * { animation-duration: 0.01ms !important; }
       }
  вң… Screen reader announcements for upload status
  вң… Error messages linked to form fields via aria-describedby
  вң… Loading states announced via aria-live regions
```

## 19. MOBILE & RESPONSIVE STRATEGY

```
Breakpoints (Tailwind default):
  sm:  640px  вҖ” Small phones (single column)
  md:  768px  вҖ” Large phones / tablets (2 columns)
  lg:  1024px вҖ” Tablets / small laptops (3 columns)
  xl:  1280px вҖ” Laptops (4 columns)
  2xl: 1536px вҖ” Large desktops (5 columns)

Tool Grid:
  Mobile (< 640px):  1 column, full-width cards
  Tablet (640-1024): 2 columns
  Desktop (1024+):   3-4 columns
  Large (1280+):     4-5 columns

Mobile-specific features:
  вң… Touch-friendly upload zone (large tap target)
  вң… Swipe to dismiss toasts
  вң… Bottom sheet for tool options (instead of sidebar)
  вң… Camera access for Scan to PDF tool
  вң… Native share sheet for download (Web Share API)
  вң… PWA manifest for add-to-home-screen
  вң… Touch scroll for category tabs (overflow-x: auto)
```

## QUICK START COMMANDS

```bash
# Clone and setup
git clone https://github.com/yourusername/ishu-tools
cd ishu-tools
pnpm install

# Setup database
cd apps/api
npx prisma migrate dev --name init
npx prisma db seed

# Start development
pnpm dev                    # Starts both web + api
# OR separately:
cd apps/web && pnpm dev     # Frontend: http://localhost:3000
cd apps/api && pnpm dev     # Backend: http://localhost:3001

# Build for production
pnpm build                  # Builds all packages

# Deploy frontend
cd apps/web && vercel --prod

# Deploy backend
cd apps/api && git push render main
```
